2016 
2017 Node*
2018 LibraryCallKit::generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id, Node* x0, Node* y0) {
2019   // These are the candidate return value:
2020   Node* xvalue = x0;
2021   Node* yvalue = y0;
2022 
2023   if (xvalue == yvalue) {
2024     return xvalue;
2025   }
2026 
2027   bool want_max = (id == vmIntrinsics::_max);
2028 
2029   const TypeInt* txvalue = _gvn.type(xvalue)->isa_int();
2030   const TypeInt* tyvalue = _gvn.type(yvalue)->isa_int();
2031   if (txvalue == NULL || tyvalue == NULL)  return top();
2032   // This is not really necessary, but it is consistent with a
2033   // hypothetical MaxINode::Value method:
2034   int widen = MAX2(txvalue->_widen, tyvalue->_widen);
2035 
2036   // %%% This folding logic should (ideally) be in a different place.
2037   // Some should be inside IfNode, and there to be a more reliable
2038   // transformation of ?: style patterns into cmoves.  We also want
2039   // more powerful optimizations around cmove and min/max.
2040 
2041   // Try to find a dominating comparison of these guys.
2042   // It can simplify the index computation for Arrays.copyOf
2043   // and similar uses of System.arraycopy.
2044   // First, compute the normalized version of CmpI(x, y).
2045   int   cmp_op = Op_CmpI;
2046   Node* xkey = xvalue;
2047   Node* ykey = yvalue;
2048   Node* ideal_cmpxy = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(xkey, ykey));
2049   if (ideal_cmpxy->is_Cmp()) {
2050     // E.g., if we have CmpI(length - offset, count),
2051     // it might idealize to CmpI(length, count + offset)
2052     cmp_op = ideal_cmpxy->Opcode();
2053     xkey = ideal_cmpxy->in(1);
2054     ykey = ideal_cmpxy->in(2);
2055   }
2056 
2057   // Start by locating any relevant comparisons.
2058   Node* start_from = (xkey->outcnt() < ykey->outcnt()) ? xkey : ykey;
2059   Node* cmpxy = NULL;
2060   Node* cmpyx = NULL;
2061   for (DUIterator_Fast kmax, k = start_from->fast_outs(kmax); k < kmax; k++) {
2062     Node* cmp = start_from->fast_out(k);
2063     if (cmp->outcnt() > 0 &&            // must have prior uses
2064         cmp->in(0) == NULL &&           // must be context-independent
2065         cmp->Opcode() == cmp_op) {      // right kind of compare
2066       if (cmp->in(1) == xkey && cmp->in(2) == ykey)  cmpxy = cmp;
2067       if (cmp->in(1) == ykey && cmp->in(2) == xkey)  cmpyx = cmp;
2068     }
2069   }
2070 
2071   const int NCMPS = 2;
2072   Node* cmps[NCMPS] = { cmpxy, cmpyx };
2073   int cmpn;
2074   for (cmpn = 0; cmpn < NCMPS; cmpn++) {
2075     if (cmps[cmpn] != NULL)  break;     // find a result
2076   }
2077   if (cmpn < NCMPS) {
2078     // Look for a dominating test that tells us the min and max.
2079     int depth = 0;                // Limit search depth for speed
2080     Node* dom = control();
2081     for (; dom != NULL; dom = IfNode::up_one_dom(dom, true)) {
2082       if (++depth >= 100)  break;
2083       Node* ifproj = dom;
2084       if (!ifproj->is_Proj())  continue;
2085       Node* iff = ifproj->in(0);
2086       if (!iff->is_If())  continue;
2087       Node* bol = iff->in(1);
2088       if (!bol->is_Bool())  continue;
2089       Node* cmp = bol->in(1);
2090       if (cmp == NULL)  continue;
2091       for (cmpn = 0; cmpn < NCMPS; cmpn++)
2092         if (cmps[cmpn] == cmp)  break;
2093       if (cmpn == NCMPS)  continue;
2094       BoolTest::mask btest = bol->as_Bool()->_test._test;
2095       if (ifproj->is_IfFalse())  btest = BoolTest(btest).negate();
2096       if (cmp->in(1) == ykey)    btest = BoolTest(btest).commute();
2097       // At this point, we know that 'x btest y' is true.
2098       switch (btest) {
2099       case BoolTest::eq:
2100         // They are proven equal, so we can collapse the min/max.
2101         // Either value is the answer.  Choose the simpler.
2102         if (is_simple_name(yvalue) && !is_simple_name(xvalue))
2103           return yvalue;
2104         return xvalue;
2105       case BoolTest::lt:          // x < y
2106       case BoolTest::le:          // x <= y
2107         return (want_max ? yvalue : xvalue);
2108       case BoolTest::gt:          // x > y
2109       case BoolTest::ge:          // x >= y
2110         return (want_max ? xvalue : yvalue);
2111       default:
2112         break;
2113       }
2114     }
2115   }
2116 
2117   // We failed to find a dominating test.
2118   // Let's pick a test that might GVN with prior tests.
2119   Node*          best_bol   = NULL;
2120   BoolTest::mask best_btest = BoolTest::illegal;
2121   for (cmpn = 0; cmpn < NCMPS; cmpn++) {
2122     Node* cmp = cmps[cmpn];
2123     if (cmp == NULL)  continue;
2124     for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = cmp->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
2125       Node* bol = cmp->fast_out(j);
2126       if (!bol->is_Bool())  continue;
2127       BoolTest::mask btest = bol->as_Bool()->_test._test;
2128       if (btest == BoolTest::eq || btest == BoolTest::ne)  continue;
2129       if (cmp->in(1) == ykey)   btest = BoolTest(btest).commute();
2130       if (bol->outcnt() > (best_bol == NULL ? 0 : best_bol->outcnt())) {
2131         best_bol   = bol->as_Bool();
2132         best_btest = btest;
2133       }
2134     }
2135   }
2136 
2137   Node* answer_if_true  = NULL;
2138   Node* answer_if_false = NULL;
2139   switch (best_btest) {
2140   default:
2141     if (cmpxy == NULL)
2142       cmpxy = ideal_cmpxy;
2143     best_bol = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpxy, BoolTest::lt));
2144     // and fall through:
2145   case BoolTest::lt:          // x < y
2146   case BoolTest::le:          // x <= y
2147     answer_if_true  = (want_max ? yvalue : xvalue);
2148     answer_if_false = (want_max ? xvalue : yvalue);
2149     break;
2150   case BoolTest::gt:          // x > y
2151   case BoolTest::ge:          // x >= y
2152     answer_if_true  = (want_max ? xvalue : yvalue);
2153     answer_if_false = (want_max ? yvalue : xvalue);
2154     break;
2155   }
2156 
2157   jint hi, lo;
2158   if (want_max) {
2159     // We can sharpen the minimum.
2160     hi = MAX2(txvalue->_hi, tyvalue->_hi);
2161     lo = MAX2(txvalue->_lo, tyvalue->_lo);
2162   } else {
2163     // We can sharpen the maximum.
2164     hi = MIN2(txvalue->_hi, tyvalue->_hi);
2165     lo = MIN2(txvalue->_lo, tyvalue->_lo);
2166   }
2167 
2168   // Use a flow-free graph structure, to avoid creating excess control edges
2169   // which could hinder other optimizations.
2170   // Since Math.min/max is often used with arraycopy, we want
2171   // tightly_coupled_allocation to be able to see beyond min/max expressions.
2172   Node* cmov = CMoveNode::make(NULL, best_bol,
2173                                answer_if_false, answer_if_true,
2174                                TypeInt::make(lo, hi, widen));
2175 
2176   return _gvn.transform(cmov);
2177 
2178   /*
2179   // This is not as desirable as it may seem, since Min and Max
2180   // nodes do not have a full set of optimizations.
2181   // And they would interfere, anyway, with 'if' optimizations
2182   // and with CMoveI canonical forms.
2183   switch (id) {
2184   case vmIntrinsics::_min:
2185     result_val = _gvn.transform(new (C, 3) MinINode(x,y)); break;
2186   case vmIntrinsics::_max:
2187     result_val = _gvn.transform(new (C, 3) MaxINode(x,y)); break;
2188   default:
2189     ShouldNotReachHere();
2190   }
2191   */
2192 }
2193 
2194 inline int
2195 LibraryCallKit::classify_unsafe_addr(Node* &base, Node* &offset, BasicType type) {
2196   const TypePtr* base_type = TypePtr::NULL_PTR;
2197   if (base != NULL)  base_type = _gvn.type(base)->isa_ptr();
2198   if (base_type == NULL) {
2199     // Unknown type.
2200     return Type::AnyPtr;
2201   } else if (base_type == TypePtr::NULL_PTR) {
2202     // Since this is a NULL+long form, we have to switch to a rawptr.
2203     base   = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(offset));
2204     offset = MakeConX(0);
2205     return Type::RawPtr;
2206   } else if (base_type->base() == Type::RawPtr) {
2207     return Type::RawPtr;
2208   } else if (base_type->isa_oopptr()) {
2209     // Base is never null => always a heap address.
2210     if (!TypePtr::NULL_PTR->higher_equal(base_type)) {
2211       return Type::OopPtr;
2212     }
2213     // Offset is small => always a heap address.
2214     const TypeX* offset_type = _gvn.type(offset)->isa_intptr_t();
2215     if (offset_type != NULL &&
2216         base_type->offset() == 0 &&     // (should always be?)
2217         offset_type->_lo >= 0 &&
2218         !MacroAssembler::needs_explicit_null_check(offset_type->_hi)) {
2219       return Type::OopPtr;
2220     } else if (type == T_OBJECT) {
2221       // off heap access to an oop doesn't make any sense. Has to be on
2222       // heap.
2223       return Type::OopPtr;
2224     }
2225     // Otherwise, it might either be oop+off or NULL+addr.
2226     return Type::AnyPtr;
2227   } else {
2228     // No information:
2229     return Type::AnyPtr;
2230   }
2231 }
2232 
2233 inline Node* LibraryCallKit::make_unsafe_address(Node*& base, Node* offset, DecoratorSet decorators, BasicType type, bool can_cast) {
2234   Node* uncasted_base = base;
2235   int kind = classify_unsafe_addr(uncasted_base, offset, type);
2236   if (kind == Type::RawPtr) {
2237     return basic_plus_adr(top(), uncasted_base, offset);
2238   } else if (kind == Type::AnyPtr) {
2239     assert(base == uncasted_base, "unexpected base change");
2240     if (can_cast) {
2241       if (!_gvn.type(base)->speculative_maybe_null() &&
2242           !too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_speculate_null_check)) {
2243         // According to profiling, this access is always on
2244         // heap. Casting the base to not null and thus avoiding membars
2245         // around the access should allow better optimizations
2246         Node* null_ctl = top();
2247         base = null_check_oop(base, &null_ctl, true, true, true);
2248         assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
2249         return basic_plus_adr(base, offset);
2250       } else if (_gvn.type(base)->speculative_always_null() &&
2251                  !too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_speculate_null_assert)) {
2252         // According to profiling, this access is always off
2253         // heap.
2254         base = null_assert(base);
2255         Node* raw_base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(offset));
2256         offset = MakeConX(0);
2257         return basic_plus_adr(top(), raw_base, offset);
2258       }
2259     }
2260     // We don't know if it's an on heap or off heap access. Fall back
2261     // to raw memory access.
2262     Node* raw = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), base, TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM));
2263     return basic_plus_adr(top(), raw, offset);
2264   } else {
2265     assert(base == uncasted_base, "unexpected base change");
2266     // We know it's an on heap access so base can't be null
2267     if (TypePtr::NULL_PTR->higher_equal(_gvn.type(base))) {
2268       base = must_be_not_null(base, true);
2269     }
2270     return basic_plus_adr(base, offset);
2271   }
2272 }
2273 
2274 //--------------------------inline_number_methods-----------------------------
2275 // inline int     Integer.numberOfLeadingZeros(int)
2276 // inline int        Long.numberOfLeadingZeros(long)
2277 //
2278 // inline int     Integer.numberOfTrailingZeros(int)
2279 // inline int        Long.numberOfTrailingZeros(long)
2280 //
2281 // inline int     Integer.bitCount(int)
2282 // inline int        Long.bitCount(long)
2283 //
2284 // inline char  Character.reverseBytes(char)
2285 // inline short     Short.reverseBytes(short)
2286 // inline int     Integer.reverseBytes(int)
2287 // inline long       Long.reverseBytes(long)
2288 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_number_methods(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
2289   Node* arg = argument(0);
2290   Node* n = NULL;
2291   switch (id) {
2292   case vmIntrinsics::_numberOfLeadingZeros_i:   n = new CountLeadingZerosINode( arg);  break;
2293   case vmIntrinsics::_numberOfLeadingZeros_l:   n = new CountLeadingZerosLNode( arg);  break;
2294   case vmIntrinsics::_numberOfTrailingZeros_i:  n = new CountTrailingZerosINode(arg);  break;
2295   case vmIntrinsics::_numberOfTrailingZeros_l:  n = new CountTrailingZerosLNode(arg);  break;
2296   case vmIntrinsics::_bitCount_i:               n = new PopCountINode(          arg);  break;
2297   case vmIntrinsics::_bitCount_l:               n = new PopCountLNode(          arg);  break;
2298   case vmIntrinsics::_reverseBytes_c:           n = new ReverseBytesUSNode(0,   arg);  break;
2299   case vmIntrinsics::_reverseBytes_s:           n = new ReverseBytesSNode( 0,   arg);  break;
2300   case vmIntrinsics::_reverseBytes_i:           n = new ReverseBytesINode( 0,   arg);  break;
2301   case vmIntrinsics::_reverseBytes_l:           n = new ReverseBytesLNode( 0,   arg);  break;
2302   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
2303   }
2304   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
2305   return true;
2306 }
2307 
2308 //----------------------------inline_unsafe_access----------------------------
2309 
2310 const TypeOopPtr* LibraryCallKit::sharpen_unsafe_type(Compile::AliasType* alias_type, const TypePtr *adr_type) {
2311   // Attempt to infer a sharper value type from the offset and base type.
2312   ciKlass* sharpened_klass = NULL;
2313 
2314   // See if it is an instance field, with an object type.
2315   if (alias_type->field() != NULL) {
2316     if (alias_type->field()->type()->is_klass()) {
2317       sharpened_klass = alias_type->field()->type()->as_klass();
2318     }
2319   }
2320 
2321   // See if it is a narrow oop array.
2322   if (adr_type->isa_aryptr()) {
2323     if (adr_type->offset() >= objArrayOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes()) {
2324       const TypeOopPtr *elem_type = adr_type->is_aryptr()->elem()->isa_oopptr();
2325       if (elem_type != NULL) {
2326         sharpened_klass = elem_type->klass();
2327       }
2328     }
2329   }
2330 
2331   // The sharpened class might be unloaded if there is no class loader
2332   // contraint in place.
2333   if (sharpened_klass != NULL && sharpened_klass->is_loaded()) {
2334     const TypeOopPtr* tjp = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(sharpened_klass);
2335 
2336 #ifndef PRODUCT
2337     if (C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) {
2338       tty->print("  from base type:  ");  adr_type->dump(); tty->cr();
2339       tty->print("  sharpened value: ");  tjp->dump();      tty->cr();
2340     }
2341 #endif
2342     // Sharpen the value type.
2343     return tjp;
2344   }
2345   return NULL;
2346 }
2347 
2348 DecoratorSet LibraryCallKit::mo_decorator_for_access_kind(AccessKind kind) {
2349   switch (kind) {
2350       case Relaxed:
2351         return MO_UNORDERED;
2352       case Opaque:
2353         return MO_RELAXED;
2354       case Acquire:
2355         return MO_ACQUIRE;
2356       case Release:
2357         return MO_RELEASE;
2358       case Volatile:
2359         return MO_SEQ_CST;
2360       default:
2361         ShouldNotReachHere();
2362         return 0;
2363   }
2364 }
2365 
2366 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_access(bool is_store, const BasicType type, const AccessKind kind, const bool unaligned) {
2367   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
2368   DecoratorSet decorators = C2_UNSAFE_ACCESS;
2369   guarantee(!is_store || kind != Acquire, "Acquire accesses can be produced only for loads");
2370   guarantee( is_store || kind != Release, "Release accesses can be produced only for stores");
2371   assert(type != T_OBJECT || !unaligned, "unaligned access not supported with object type");
2372 
2373   if (is_reference_type(type)) {
2374     decorators |= ON_UNKNOWN_OOP_REF;
2375   }
2376 
2377   if (unaligned) {
2378     decorators |= C2_UNALIGNED;
2379   }
2380 
2381 #ifndef PRODUCT
2382   {
2383     ResourceMark rm;
2384     // Check the signatures.
2385     ciSignature* sig = callee()->signature();
2386 #ifdef ASSERT
2387     if (!is_store) {
2388       // Object getReference(Object base, int/long offset), etc.
2389       BasicType rtype = sig->return_type()->basic_type();
2390       assert(rtype == type, "getter must return the expected value");
2391       assert(sig->count() == 2, "oop getter has 2 arguments");
2392       assert(sig->type_at(0)->basic_type() == T_OBJECT, "getter base is object");
2393       assert(sig->type_at(1)->basic_type() == T_LONG, "getter offset is correct");
2394     } else {
2395       // void putReference(Object base, int/long offset, Object x), etc.
2396       assert(sig->return_type()->basic_type() == T_VOID, "putter must not return a value");
2397       assert(sig->count() == 3, "oop putter has 3 arguments");
2398       assert(sig->type_at(0)->basic_type() == T_OBJECT, "putter base is object");
2399       assert(sig->type_at(1)->basic_type() == T_LONG, "putter offset is correct");
2400       BasicType vtype = sig->type_at(sig->count()-1)->basic_type();
2401       assert(vtype == type, "putter must accept the expected value");
2402     }
2403 #endif // ASSERT
2404  }
2405 #endif //PRODUCT
2406 
2407   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
2408 
2409   Node* receiver = argument(0);  // type: oop
2410 
2411   // Build address expression.
2412   Node* adr;
2413   Node* heap_base_oop = top();
2414   Node* offset = top();
2415   Node* val;
2416 
2417   // The base is either a Java object or a value produced by Unsafe.staticFieldBase
2418   Node* base = argument(1);  // type: oop
2419   // The offset is a value produced by Unsafe.staticFieldOffset or Unsafe.objectFieldOffset
2420   offset = argument(2);  // type: long
2421   // We currently rely on the cookies produced by Unsafe.xxxFieldOffset
2422   // to be plain byte offsets, which are also the same as those accepted
2423   // by oopDesc::field_addr.
2424   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
2425          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
2426   // 32-bit machines ignore the high half!
2427   offset = ConvL2X(offset);
2428   adr = make_unsafe_address(base, offset, is_store ? ACCESS_WRITE : ACCESS_READ, type, kind == Relaxed);
2429 
2430   if (_gvn.type(base)->isa_ptr() == TypePtr::NULL_PTR) {
2431     if (type != T_OBJECT) {
2432       decorators |= IN_NATIVE; // off-heap primitive access
2433     } else {
2434       return false; // off-heap oop accesses are not supported
2435     }
2436   } else {
2437     heap_base_oop = base; // on-heap or mixed access
2438   }
2439 
2440   // Can base be NULL? Otherwise, always on-heap access.
2441   bool can_access_non_heap = TypePtr::NULL_PTR->higher_equal(_gvn.type(base));
2442 
2443   if (!can_access_non_heap) {
2444     decorators |= IN_HEAP;
2445   }
2446 
2447   val = is_store ? argument(4) : NULL;
2448 
2449   const TypePtr* adr_type = _gvn.type(adr)->isa_ptr();
2450   if (adr_type == TypePtr::NULL_PTR) {
2451     return false; // off-heap access with zero address
2452   }
2453 
2454   // Try to categorize the address.
2455   Compile::AliasType* alias_type = C->alias_type(adr_type);
2456   assert(alias_type->index() != Compile::AliasIdxBot, "no bare pointers here");
2457 
2458   if (alias_type->adr_type() == TypeInstPtr::KLASS ||
2459       alias_type->adr_type() == TypeAryPtr::RANGE) {
2460     return false; // not supported
2461   }
2462 
2463   bool mismatched = false;
2464   BasicType bt = alias_type->basic_type();
2465   if (bt != T_ILLEGAL) {
2466     assert(alias_type->adr_type()->is_oopptr(), "should be on-heap access");
2467     if (bt == T_BYTE && adr_type->isa_aryptr()) {
2468       // Alias type doesn't differentiate between byte[] and boolean[]).
2469       // Use address type to get the element type.
2470       bt = adr_type->is_aryptr()->elem()->array_element_basic_type();
2471     }
2472     if (bt == T_ARRAY || bt == T_NARROWOOP) {
2473       // accessing an array field with getReference is not a mismatch
2474       bt = T_OBJECT;
2475     }
2476     if ((bt == T_OBJECT) != (type == T_OBJECT)) {
2477       // Don't intrinsify mismatched object accesses
2478       return false;
2479     }
2480     mismatched = (bt != type);
2481   } else if (alias_type->adr_type()->isa_oopptr()) {
2482     mismatched = true; // conservatively mark all "wide" on-heap accesses as mismatched
2483   }
2484 
2485   assert(!mismatched || alias_type->adr_type()->is_oopptr(), "off-heap access can't be mismatched");
2486 
2487   if (mismatched) {
2488     decorators |= C2_MISMATCHED;
2489   }
2490 
2491   // First guess at the value type.
2492   const Type *value_type = Type::get_const_basic_type(type);
2493 
2494   // Figure out the memory ordering.
2495   decorators |= mo_decorator_for_access_kind(kind);
2496 
2497   if (!is_store && type == T_OBJECT) {
2498     const TypeOopPtr* tjp = sharpen_unsafe_type(alias_type, adr_type);
2499     if (tjp != NULL) {
2500       value_type = tjp;
2501     }
2502   }
2503 
2504   receiver = null_check(receiver);
2505   if (stopped()) {
2506     return true;
2507   }
2508   // Heap pointers get a null-check from the interpreter,
2509   // as a courtesy.  However, this is not guaranteed by Unsafe,
2510   // and it is not possible to fully distinguish unintended nulls
2511   // from intended ones in this API.
2512 
2513   if (!is_store) {
2514     Node* p = NULL;
2515     // Try to constant fold a load from a constant field
2516     ciField* field = alias_type->field();
2517     if (heap_base_oop != top() && field != NULL && field->is_constant() && !mismatched) {
2518       // final or stable field
2519       p = make_constant_from_field(field, heap_base_oop);
2520     }
2521 
2522     if (p == NULL) { // Could not constant fold the load
2523       p = access_load_at(heap_base_oop, adr, adr_type, value_type, type, decorators);
2524       // Normalize the value returned by getBoolean in the following cases
2525       if (type == T_BOOLEAN &&
2526           (mismatched ||
2527            heap_base_oop == top() ||                  // - heap_base_oop is NULL or
2528            (can_access_non_heap && field == NULL))    // - heap_base_oop is potentially NULL
2529                                                       //   and the unsafe access is made to large offset
2530                                                       //   (i.e., larger than the maximum offset necessary for any
2531                                                       //   field access)
2532             ) {
2533           IdealKit ideal = IdealKit(this);
2534 #define __ ideal.
2535           IdealVariable normalized_result(ideal);
2536           __ declarations_done();
2537           __ set(normalized_result, p);
2538           __ if_then(p, BoolTest::ne, ideal.ConI(0));
2539           __ set(normalized_result, ideal.ConI(1));
2540           ideal.end_if();
2541           final_sync(ideal);
2542           p = __ value(normalized_result);
2543 #undef __
2544       }
2545     }
2546     if (type == T_ADDRESS) {
2547       p = gvn().transform(new CastP2XNode(NULL, p));
2548       p = ConvX2UL(p);
2549     }
2550     // The load node has the control of the preceding MemBarCPUOrder.  All
2551     // following nodes will have the control of the MemBarCPUOrder inserted at
2552     // the end of this method.  So, pushing the load onto the stack at a later
2553     // point is fine.
2554     set_result(p);
2555   } else {
2556     if (bt == T_ADDRESS) {
2557       // Repackage the long as a pointer.
2558       val = ConvL2X(val);
2559       val = gvn().transform(new CastX2PNode(val));
2560     }
2561     access_store_at(heap_base_oop, adr, adr_type, val, value_type, type, decorators);
2562   }
2563 
2564   return true;
2565 }
2566 
2567 //----------------------------inline_unsafe_load_store----------------------------
2568 // This method serves a couple of different customers (depending on LoadStoreKind):
2569 //
2570 // LS_cmp_swap:
2571 //
2572 //   boolean compareAndSetReference(Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2573 //   boolean compareAndSetInt(   Object o, long offset, int    expected, int    x);
2574 //   boolean compareAndSetLong(  Object o, long offset, long   expected, long   x);
2575 //
2576 // LS_cmp_swap_weak:
2577 //
2578 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetReference(       Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2579 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetReferencePlain(  Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2580 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetReferenceAcquire(Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2581 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetReferenceRelease(Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2582 //
2583 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetInt(          Object o, long offset, int    expected, int    x);
2584 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetIntPlain(     Object o, long offset, int    expected, int    x);
2585 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetIntAcquire(   Object o, long offset, int    expected, int    x);
2586 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetIntRelease(   Object o, long offset, int    expected, int    x);
2587 //
2588 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetLong(         Object o, long offset, long   expected, long   x);
2589 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetLongPlain(    Object o, long offset, long   expected, long   x);
2590 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetLongAcquire(  Object o, long offset, long   expected, long   x);
2591 //   boolean weakCompareAndSetLongRelease(  Object o, long offset, long   expected, long   x);
2592 //
2593 // LS_cmp_exchange:
2594 //
2595 //   Object compareAndExchangeReferenceVolatile(Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2596 //   Object compareAndExchangeReferenceAcquire( Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2597 //   Object compareAndExchangeReferenceRelease( Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2598 //
2599 //   Object compareAndExchangeIntVolatile(   Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2600 //   Object compareAndExchangeIntAcquire(    Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2601 //   Object compareAndExchangeIntRelease(    Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2602 //
2603 //   Object compareAndExchangeLongVolatile(  Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2604 //   Object compareAndExchangeLongAcquire(   Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2605 //   Object compareAndExchangeLongRelease(   Object o, long offset, Object expected, Object x);
2606 //
2607 // LS_get_add:
2608 //
2609 //   int  getAndAddInt( Object o, long offset, int  delta)
2610 //   long getAndAddLong(Object o, long offset, long delta)
2611 //
2612 // LS_get_set:
2613 //
2614 //   int    getAndSet(Object o, long offset, int    newValue)
2615 //   long   getAndSet(Object o, long offset, long   newValue)
2616 //   Object getAndSet(Object o, long offset, Object newValue)
2617 //
2618 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_load_store(const BasicType type, const LoadStoreKind kind, const AccessKind access_kind) {
2619   // This basic scheme here is the same as inline_unsafe_access, but
2620   // differs in enough details that combining them would make the code
2621   // overly confusing.  (This is a true fact! I originally combined
2622   // them, but even I was confused by it!) As much code/comments as
2623   // possible are retained from inline_unsafe_access though to make
2624   // the correspondences clearer. - dl
2625 
2626   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
2627 
2628   DecoratorSet decorators = C2_UNSAFE_ACCESS;
2629   decorators |= mo_decorator_for_access_kind(access_kind);
2630 
2631 #ifndef PRODUCT
2632   BasicType rtype;
2633   {
2634     ResourceMark rm;
2635     // Check the signatures.
2636     ciSignature* sig = callee()->signature();
2637     rtype = sig->return_type()->basic_type();
2638     switch(kind) {
2639       case LS_get_add:
2640       case LS_get_set: {
2641       // Check the signatures.
2642 #ifdef ASSERT
2643       assert(rtype == type, "get and set must return the expected type");
2644       assert(sig->count() == 3, "get and set has 3 arguments");
2645       assert(sig->type_at(0)->basic_type() == T_OBJECT, "get and set base is object");
2646       assert(sig->type_at(1)->basic_type() == T_LONG, "get and set offset is long");
2647       assert(sig->type_at(2)->basic_type() == type, "get and set must take expected type as new value/delta");
2648       assert(access_kind == Volatile, "mo is not passed to intrinsic nodes in current implementation");
2649 #endif // ASSERT
2650         break;
2651       }
2652       case LS_cmp_swap:
2653       case LS_cmp_swap_weak: {
2654       // Check the signatures.
2655 #ifdef ASSERT
2656       assert(rtype == T_BOOLEAN, "CAS must return boolean");
2657       assert(sig->count() == 4, "CAS has 4 arguments");
2658       assert(sig->type_at(0)->basic_type() == T_OBJECT, "CAS base is object");
2659       assert(sig->type_at(1)->basic_type() == T_LONG, "CAS offset is long");
2660 #endif // ASSERT
2661         break;
2662       }
2663       case LS_cmp_exchange: {
2664       // Check the signatures.
2665 #ifdef ASSERT
2666       assert(rtype == type, "CAS must return the expected type");
2667       assert(sig->count() == 4, "CAS has 4 arguments");
2668       assert(sig->type_at(0)->basic_type() == T_OBJECT, "CAS base is object");
2669       assert(sig->type_at(1)->basic_type() == T_LONG, "CAS offset is long");
2670 #endif // ASSERT
2671         break;
2672       }
2673       default:
2674         ShouldNotReachHere();
2675     }
2676   }
2677 #endif //PRODUCT
2678 
2679   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
2680 
2681   // Get arguments:
2682   Node* receiver = NULL;
2683   Node* base     = NULL;
2684   Node* offset   = NULL;
2685   Node* oldval   = NULL;
2686   Node* newval   = NULL;
2687   switch(kind) {
2688     case LS_cmp_swap:
2689     case LS_cmp_swap_weak:
2690     case LS_cmp_exchange: {
2691       const bool two_slot_type = type2size[type] == 2;
2692       receiver = argument(0);  // type: oop
2693       base     = argument(1);  // type: oop
2694       offset   = argument(2);  // type: long
2695       oldval   = argument(4);  // type: oop, int, or long
2696       newval   = argument(two_slot_type ? 6 : 5);  // type: oop, int, or long
2697       break;
2698     }
2699     case LS_get_add:
2700     case LS_get_set: {
2701       receiver = argument(0);  // type: oop
2702       base     = argument(1);  // type: oop
2703       offset   = argument(2);  // type: long
2704       oldval   = NULL;
2705       newval   = argument(4);  // type: oop, int, or long
2706       break;
2707     }
2708     default:
2709       ShouldNotReachHere();
2710   }
2711 
2712   // Build field offset expression.
2713   // We currently rely on the cookies produced by Unsafe.xxxFieldOffset
2714   // to be plain byte offsets, which are also the same as those accepted
2715   // by oopDesc::field_addr.
2716   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11, "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
2717   // 32-bit machines ignore the high half of long offsets
2718   offset = ConvL2X(offset);
2719   Node* adr = make_unsafe_address(base, offset, ACCESS_WRITE | ACCESS_READ, type, false);
2720   const TypePtr *adr_type = _gvn.type(adr)->isa_ptr();
2721 
2722   Compile::AliasType* alias_type = C->alias_type(adr_type);
2723   BasicType bt = alias_type->basic_type();
2724   if (bt != T_ILLEGAL &&
2725       (is_reference_type(bt) != (type == T_OBJECT))) {
2726     // Don't intrinsify mismatched object accesses.
2727     return false;
2728   }
2729 
2730   // For CAS, unlike inline_unsafe_access, there seems no point in
2731   // trying to refine types. Just use the coarse types here.
2732   assert(alias_type->index() != Compile::AliasIdxBot, "no bare pointers here");
2733   const Type *value_type = Type::get_const_basic_type(type);
2734 
2735   switch (kind) {
2736     case LS_get_set:
2737     case LS_cmp_exchange: {
2738       if (type == T_OBJECT) {
2739         const TypeOopPtr* tjp = sharpen_unsafe_type(alias_type, adr_type);
2740         if (tjp != NULL) {
2741           value_type = tjp;
2742         }
2743       }
2744       break;
2745     }
2746     case LS_cmp_swap:
2747     case LS_cmp_swap_weak:
2748     case LS_get_add:
2749       break;
2750     default:
2751       ShouldNotReachHere();
2752   }
2753 
2754   // Null check receiver.
2755   receiver = null_check(receiver);
2756   if (stopped()) {
2757     return true;
2758   }
2759 
2760   int alias_idx = C->get_alias_index(adr_type);
2761 
2762   if (is_reference_type(type)) {
2763     decorators |= IN_HEAP | ON_UNKNOWN_OOP_REF;
2764 
2765     // Transformation of a value which could be NULL pointer (CastPP #NULL)
2766     // could be delayed during Parse (for example, in adjust_map_after_if()).
2767     // Execute transformation here to avoid barrier generation in such case.
2768     if (_gvn.type(newval) == TypePtr::NULL_PTR)
2769       newval = _gvn.makecon(TypePtr::NULL_PTR);
2770 
2771     if (oldval != NULL && _gvn.type(oldval) == TypePtr::NULL_PTR) {
2772       // Refine the value to a null constant, when it is known to be null
2773       oldval = _gvn.makecon(TypePtr::NULL_PTR);
2774     }
2775   }
2776 
2777   Node* result = NULL;
2778   switch (kind) {
2779     case LS_cmp_exchange: {
2780       result = access_atomic_cmpxchg_val_at(base, adr, adr_type, alias_idx,
2781                                             oldval, newval, value_type, type, decorators);
2782       break;
2783     }
2784     case LS_cmp_swap_weak:
2785       decorators |= C2_WEAK_CMPXCHG;
2786     case LS_cmp_swap: {
2787       result = access_atomic_cmpxchg_bool_at(base, adr, adr_type, alias_idx,
2788                                              oldval, newval, value_type, type, decorators);
2789       break;
2790     }
2791     case LS_get_set: {
2792       result = access_atomic_xchg_at(base, adr, adr_type, alias_idx,
2793                                      newval, value_type, type, decorators);
2794       break;
2795     }
2796     case LS_get_add: {
2797       result = access_atomic_add_at(base, adr, adr_type, alias_idx,
2798                                     newval, value_type, type, decorators);
2799       break;
2800     }
2801     default:
2802       ShouldNotReachHere();
2803   }
2804 
2805   assert(type2size[result->bottom_type()->basic_type()] == type2size[rtype], "result type should match");
2806   set_result(result);
2807   return true;
2808 }
2809 
2810 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_fence(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
2811   // Regardless of form, don't allow previous ld/st to move down,
2812   // then issue acquire, release, or volatile mem_bar.
2813   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
2814   switch(id) {
2815     case vmIntrinsics::_loadFence:
2816       insert_mem_bar(Op_LoadFence);
2817       return true;
2818     case vmIntrinsics::_storeFence:
2819       insert_mem_bar(Op_StoreFence);
2820       return true;
2821     case vmIntrinsics::_fullFence:
2822       insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarVolatile);
2823       return true;
2824     default:
2825       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
2826       return false;
2827   }
2828 }
2829 
2830 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_onspinwait() {
2831   insert_mem_bar(Op_OnSpinWait);
2832   return true;
2833 }
2834 
2835 bool LibraryCallKit::klass_needs_init_guard(Node* kls) {
2836   if (!kls->is_Con()) {
2837     return true;
2838   }
2839   const TypeKlassPtr* klsptr = kls->bottom_type()->isa_klassptr();
2840   if (klsptr == NULL) {
2841     return true;
2842   }
2843   ciInstanceKlass* ik = klsptr->klass()->as_instance_klass();
2844   // don't need a guard for a klass that is already initialized
2845   return !ik->is_initialized();
2846 }
2847 
2848 //----------------------------inline_unsafe_writeback0-------------------------
2849 // public native void Unsafe.writeback0(long address)
2850 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_writeback0() {
2851   if (!Matcher::has_match_rule(Op_CacheWB)) {
2852     return false;
2853   }
2854 #ifndef PRODUCT
2855   assert(Matcher::has_match_rule(Op_CacheWBPreSync), "found match rule for CacheWB but not CacheWBPreSync");
2856   assert(Matcher::has_match_rule(Op_CacheWBPostSync), "found match rule for CacheWB but not CacheWBPostSync");
2857   ciSignature* sig = callee()->signature();
2858   assert(sig->type_at(0)->basic_type() == T_LONG, "Unsafe_writeback0 address is long!");
2859 #endif
2860   null_check_receiver();  // null-check, then ignore
2861   Node *addr = argument(1);
2862   addr = new CastX2PNode(addr);
2863   addr = _gvn.transform(addr);
2864   Node *flush = new CacheWBNode(control(), memory(TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM), addr);
2865   flush = _gvn.transform(flush);
2866   set_memory(flush, TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM);
2867   return true;
2868 }
2869 
2870 //----------------------------inline_unsafe_writeback0-------------------------
2871 // public native void Unsafe.writeback0(long address)
2872 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_writebackSync0(bool is_pre) {
2873   if (is_pre && !Matcher::has_match_rule(Op_CacheWBPreSync)) {
2874     return false;
2875   }
2876   if (!is_pre && !Matcher::has_match_rule(Op_CacheWBPostSync)) {
2877     return false;
2878   }
2879 #ifndef PRODUCT
2880   assert(Matcher::has_match_rule(Op_CacheWB),
2881          (is_pre ? "found match rule for CacheWBPreSync but not CacheWB"
2882                 : "found match rule for CacheWBPostSync but not CacheWB"));
2883 
2884 #endif
2885   null_check_receiver();  // null-check, then ignore
2886   Node *sync;
2887   if (is_pre) {
2888     sync = new CacheWBPreSyncNode(control(), memory(TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM));
2889   } else {
2890     sync = new CacheWBPostSyncNode(control(), memory(TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM));
2891   }
2892   sync = _gvn.transform(sync);
2893   set_memory(sync, TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM);
2894   return true;
2895 }
2896 
2897 //----------------------------inline_unsafe_allocate---------------------------
2898 // public native Object Unsafe.allocateInstance(Class<?> cls);
2899 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_allocate() {
2900   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
2901 
2902   null_check_receiver();  // null-check, then ignore
2903   Node* cls = null_check(argument(1));
2904   if (stopped())  return true;
2905 
2906   Node* kls = load_klass_from_mirror(cls, false, NULL, 0);
2907   kls = null_check(kls);
2908   if (stopped())  return true;  // argument was like int.class
2909 
2910   Node* test = NULL;
2911   if (LibraryCallKit::klass_needs_init_guard(kls)) {
2912     // Note:  The argument might still be an illegal value like
2913     // Serializable.class or Object[].class.   The runtime will handle it.
2914     // But we must make an explicit check for initialization.
2915     Node* insp = basic_plus_adr(kls, in_bytes(InstanceKlass::init_state_offset()));
2916     // Use T_BOOLEAN for InstanceKlass::_init_state so the compiler
2917     // can generate code to load it as unsigned byte.
2918     Node* inst = make_load(NULL, insp, TypeInt::UBYTE, T_BOOLEAN, MemNode::unordered);
2919     Node* bits = intcon(InstanceKlass::fully_initialized);
2920     test = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(inst, bits));
2921     // The 'test' is non-zero if we need to take a slow path.
2922   }
2923 
2924   Node* obj = new_instance(kls, test);
2925   set_result(obj);
2926   return true;
2927 }
2928 
2929 //------------------------inline_native_time_funcs--------------
2930 // inline code for System.currentTimeMillis() and System.nanoTime()
2931 // these have the same type and signature
2932 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_time_funcs(address funcAddr, const char* funcName) {
2933   const TypeFunc* tf = OptoRuntime::void_long_Type();
2934   const TypePtr* no_memory_effects = NULL;
2935   Node* time = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, tf, funcAddr, funcName, no_memory_effects);
2936   Node* value = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(time, TypeFunc::Parms+0));
2937 #ifdef ASSERT
2938   Node* value_top = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(time, TypeFunc::Parms+1));
2939   assert(value_top == top(), "second value must be top");
2940 #endif
2941   set_result(value);
2942   return true;
2943 }
2944 
2945 #ifdef JFR_HAVE_INTRINSICS
2946 
2947 /*
2948 * oop -> myklass
2949 * myklass->trace_id |= USED
2950 * return myklass->trace_id & ~0x3
2951 */
2952 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_classID() {
2953   Node* cls = null_check(argument(0), T_OBJECT);
2954   Node* kls = load_klass_from_mirror(cls, false, NULL, 0);
2955   kls = null_check(kls, T_OBJECT);
2956 
2957   ByteSize offset = KLASS_TRACE_ID_OFFSET;
2958   Node* insp = basic_plus_adr(kls, in_bytes(offset));
2959   Node* tvalue = make_load(NULL, insp, TypeLong::LONG, T_LONG, MemNode::unordered);
2960 
2961   Node* clsused = longcon(0x01l); // set the class bit
2962   Node* orl = _gvn.transform(new OrLNode(tvalue, clsused));
2963   const TypePtr *adr_type = _gvn.type(insp)->isa_ptr();
2964   store_to_memory(control(), insp, orl, T_LONG, adr_type, MemNode::unordered);
2965 
2966 #ifdef TRACE_ID_META_BITS
2967   Node* mbits = longcon(~TRACE_ID_META_BITS);
2968   tvalue = _gvn.transform(new AndLNode(tvalue, mbits));
2969 #endif
2970 #ifdef TRACE_ID_SHIFT
2971   Node* cbits = intcon(TRACE_ID_SHIFT);
2972   tvalue = _gvn.transform(new URShiftLNode(tvalue, cbits));
2973 #endif
2974 
2975   set_result(tvalue);
2976   return true;
2977 
2978 }
2979 
2980 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getEventWriter() {
2981   Node* tls_ptr = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
2982 
2983   Node* jobj_ptr = basic_plus_adr(top(), tls_ptr,
2984                                   in_bytes(THREAD_LOCAL_WRITER_OFFSET_JFR));
2985 
2986   Node* jobj = make_load(control(), jobj_ptr, TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
2987 
2988   Node* jobj_cmp_null = _gvn.transform( new CmpPNode(jobj, null()) );
2989   Node* test_jobj_eq_null  = _gvn.transform( new BoolNode(jobj_cmp_null, BoolTest::eq) );
2990 
2991   IfNode* iff_jobj_null =
2992     create_and_map_if(control(), test_jobj_eq_null, PROB_MIN, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
2993 
2994   enum { _normal_path = 1,
2995          _null_path = 2,
2996          PATH_LIMIT };
2997 
2998   RegionNode* result_rgn = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
2999   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_rgn, TypeInstPtr::BOTTOM);
3000 
3001   Node* jobj_is_null = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(iff_jobj_null));
3002   result_rgn->init_req(_null_path, jobj_is_null);
3003   result_val->init_req(_null_path, null());
3004 
3005   Node* jobj_is_not_null = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(iff_jobj_null));
3006   set_control(jobj_is_not_null);
3007   Node* res = access_load(jobj, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL, T_OBJECT,
3008                           IN_NATIVE | C2_CONTROL_DEPENDENT_LOAD);
3009   result_rgn->init_req(_normal_path, control());
3010   result_val->init_req(_normal_path, res);
3011 
3012   set_result(result_rgn, result_val);
3013 
3014   return true;
3015 }

3017 #endif // JFR_HAVE_INTRINSICS

3019 //------------------------inline_native_currentThread------------------
3020 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_currentThread() {
3021   Node* junk = NULL;
3022   set_result(generate_current_thread(junk));
3023   return true;
3024 }
3025 
3026 //---------------------------load_mirror_from_klass----------------------------
3027 // Given a klass oop, load its java mirror (a java.lang.Class oop).
3028 Node* LibraryCallKit::load_mirror_from_klass(Node* klass) {
3029   Node* p = basic_plus_adr(klass, in_bytes(Klass::java_mirror_offset()));
3030   Node* load = make_load(NULL, p, TypeRawPtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
3031   // mirror = ((OopHandle)mirror)->resolve();
3032   return access_load(load, TypeInstPtr::MIRROR, T_OBJECT, IN_NATIVE);
3033 }
3034 
3035 //-----------------------load_klass_from_mirror_common-------------------------
3036 // Given a java mirror (a java.lang.Class oop), load its corresponding klass oop.
3037 // Test the klass oop for null (signifying a primitive Class like Integer.TYPE),
3038 // and branch to the given path on the region.
3039 // If never_see_null, take an uncommon trap on null, so we can optimistically
3040 // compile for the non-null case.
3041 // If the region is NULL, force never_see_null = true.
3042 Node* LibraryCallKit::load_klass_from_mirror_common(Node* mirror,
3043                                                     bool never_see_null,
3044                                                     RegionNode* region,
3045                                                     int null_path,
3046                                                     int offset) {
3047   if (region == NULL)  never_see_null = true;
3048   Node* p = basic_plus_adr(mirror, offset);
3049   const TypeKlassPtr*  kls_type = TypeKlassPtr::OBJECT_OR_NULL;
3050   Node* kls = _gvn.transform(LoadKlassNode::make(_gvn, NULL, immutable_memory(), p, TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM, kls_type));
3051   Node* null_ctl = top();
3052   kls = null_check_oop(kls, &null_ctl, never_see_null);
3053   if (region != NULL) {
3054     // Set region->in(null_path) if the mirror is a primitive (e.g, int.class).
3055     region->init_req(null_path, null_ctl);
3056   } else {
3057     assert(null_ctl == top(), "no loose ends");
3058   }
3059   return kls;
3060 }
3061 
3062 //--------------------(inline_native_Class_query helpers)---------------------
3063 // Use this for JVM_ACC_INTERFACE, JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST, JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER.
3064 // Fall through if (mods & mask) == bits, take the guard otherwise.
3065 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_access_flags_guard(Node* kls, int modifier_mask, int modifier_bits, RegionNode* region) {
3066   // Branch around if the given klass has the given modifier bit set.
3067   // Like generate_guard, adds a new path onto the region.
3068   Node* modp = basic_plus_adr(kls, in_bytes(Klass::access_flags_offset()));
3069   Node* mods = make_load(NULL, modp, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
3070   Node* mask = intcon(modifier_mask);
3071   Node* bits = intcon(modifier_bits);
3072   Node* mbit = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(mods, mask));
3073   Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(mbit, bits));
3074   Node* bol  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::ne));
3075   return generate_fair_guard(bol, region);
3076 }
3077 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_interface_guard(Node* kls, RegionNode* region) {
3078   return generate_access_flags_guard(kls, JVM_ACC_INTERFACE, 0, region);
3079 }
3080 
3081 //-------------------------inline_native_Class_query-------------------
3082 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Class_query(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
3083   const Type* return_type = TypeInt::BOOL;
3084   Node* prim_return_value = top();  // what happens if it's a primitive class?
3085   bool never_see_null = !too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_null_check);
3086   bool expect_prim = false;     // most of these guys expect to work on refs
3087 
3088   enum { _normal_path = 1, _prim_path = 2, PATH_LIMIT };
3089 
3090   Node* mirror = argument(0);
3091   Node* obj    = top();
3092 
3093   switch (id) {
3094   case vmIntrinsics::_isInstance:
3095     // nothing is an instance of a primitive type
3096     prim_return_value = intcon(0);
3097     obj = argument(1);
3098     break;
3099   case vmIntrinsics::_getModifiers:
3100     prim_return_value = intcon(JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT | JVM_ACC_FINAL | JVM_ACC_PUBLIC);
3101     assert(is_power_of_2((int)JVM_ACC_WRITTEN_FLAGS+1), "change next line");
3102     return_type = TypeInt::make(0, JVM_ACC_WRITTEN_FLAGS, Type::WidenMin);
3103     break;
3104   case vmIntrinsics::_isInterface:
3105     prim_return_value = intcon(0);
3106     break;
3107   case vmIntrinsics::_isArray:
3108     prim_return_value = intcon(0);
3109     expect_prim = true;  // cf. ObjectStreamClass.getClassSignature
3110     break;
3111   case vmIntrinsics::_isPrimitive:
3112     prim_return_value = intcon(1);
3113     expect_prim = true;  // obviously
3114     break;
3115   case vmIntrinsics::_getSuperclass:
3116     prim_return_value = null();
3117     return_type = TypeInstPtr::MIRROR->cast_to_ptr_type(TypePtr::BotPTR);
3118     break;
3119   case vmIntrinsics::_getClassAccessFlags:
3120     prim_return_value = intcon(JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT | JVM_ACC_FINAL | JVM_ACC_PUBLIC);
3121     return_type = TypeInt::INT;  // not bool!  6297094
3122     break;
3123   default:
3124     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
3125     break;
3126   }
3127 
3128   const TypeInstPtr* mirror_con = _gvn.type(mirror)->isa_instptr();
3129   if (mirror_con == NULL)  return false;  // cannot happen?
3130 
3131 #ifndef PRODUCT
3132   if (C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) {
3133     ciType* k = mirror_con->java_mirror_type();
3134     if (k) {
3135       tty->print("Inlining %s on constant Class ", vmIntrinsics::name_at(intrinsic_id()));
3136       k->print_name();
3137       tty->cr();
3138     }
3139   }
3140 #endif
3141 
3142   // Null-check the mirror, and the mirror's klass ptr (in case it is a primitive).
3143   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
3144   record_for_igvn(region);
3145   PhiNode* phi = new PhiNode(region, return_type);
3146 
3147   // The mirror will never be null of Reflection.getClassAccessFlags, however
3148   // it may be null for Class.isInstance or Class.getModifiers. Throw a NPE
3149   // if it is. See bug 4774291.
3150 
3151   // For Reflection.getClassAccessFlags(), the null check occurs in
3152   // the wrong place; see inline_unsafe_access(), above, for a similar
3153   // situation.
3154   mirror = null_check(mirror);
3155   // If mirror or obj is dead, only null-path is taken.
3156   if (stopped())  return true;
3157 
3158   if (expect_prim)  never_see_null = false;  // expect nulls (meaning prims)
3159 
3160   // Now load the mirror's klass metaobject, and null-check it.
3161   // Side-effects region with the control path if the klass is null.
3162   Node* kls = load_klass_from_mirror(mirror, never_see_null, region, _prim_path);
3163   // If kls is null, we have a primitive mirror.
3164   phi->init_req(_prim_path, prim_return_value);
3165   if (stopped()) { set_result(region, phi); return true; }
3166   bool safe_for_replace = (region->in(_prim_path) == top());
3167 
3168   Node* p;  // handy temp
3169   Node* null_ctl;
3170 
3171   // Now that we have the non-null klass, we can perform the real query.
3172   // For constant classes, the query will constant-fold in LoadNode::Value.
3173   Node* query_value = top();
3174   switch (id) {
3175   case vmIntrinsics::_isInstance:
3176     // nothing is an instance of a primitive type
3177     query_value = gen_instanceof(obj, kls, safe_for_replace);
3178     break;
3179 
3180   case vmIntrinsics::_getModifiers:
3181     p = basic_plus_adr(kls, in_bytes(Klass::modifier_flags_offset()));
3182     query_value = make_load(NULL, p, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
3183     break;
3184 
3185   case vmIntrinsics::_isInterface:
3186     // (To verify this code sequence, check the asserts in JVM_IsInterface.)
3187     if (generate_interface_guard(kls, region) != NULL)
3188       // A guard was added.  If the guard is taken, it was an interface.
3189       phi->add_req(intcon(1));
3190     // If we fall through, it's a plain class.
3191     query_value = intcon(0);
3192     break;
3193 
3194   case vmIntrinsics::_isArray:
3195     // (To verify this code sequence, check the asserts in JVM_IsArrayClass.)
3196     if (generate_array_guard(kls, region) != NULL)
3197       // A guard was added.  If the guard is taken, it was an array.
3198       phi->add_req(intcon(1));
3199     // If we fall through, it's a plain class.
3200     query_value = intcon(0);
3201     break;
3202 
3203   case vmIntrinsics::_isPrimitive:
3204     query_value = intcon(0); // "normal" path produces false
3205     break;
3206 
3207   case vmIntrinsics::_getSuperclass:
3208     // The rules here are somewhat unfortunate, but we can still do better
3209     // with random logic than with a JNI call.
3210     // Interfaces store null or Object as _super, but must report null.
3211     // Arrays store an intermediate super as _super, but must report Object.
3212     // Other types can report the actual _super.
3213     // (To verify this code sequence, check the asserts in JVM_IsInterface.)
3214     if (generate_interface_guard(kls, region) != NULL)
3215       // A guard was added.  If the guard is taken, it was an interface.
3216       phi->add_req(null());
3217     if (generate_array_guard(kls, region) != NULL)
3218       // A guard was added.  If the guard is taken, it was an array.
3219       phi->add_req(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(env()->Object_klass()->java_mirror())));
3220     // If we fall through, it's a plain class.  Get its _super.
3221     p = basic_plus_adr(kls, in_bytes(Klass::super_offset()));
3222     kls = _gvn.transform(LoadKlassNode::make(_gvn, NULL, immutable_memory(), p, TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM, TypeKlassPtr::OBJECT_OR_NULL));
3223     null_ctl = top();
3224     kls = null_check_oop(kls, &null_ctl);
3225     if (null_ctl != top()) {
3226       // If the guard is taken, Object.superClass is null (both klass and mirror).
3227       region->add_req(null_ctl);
3228       phi   ->add_req(null());
3229     }
3230     if (!stopped()) {
3231       query_value = load_mirror_from_klass(kls);
3232     }
3233     break;
3234 
3235   case vmIntrinsics::_getClassAccessFlags:
3236     p = basic_plus_adr(kls, in_bytes(Klass::access_flags_offset()));
3237     query_value = make_load(NULL, p, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
3238     break;
3239 
3240   default:
3241     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
3242     break;
3243   }
3244 
3245   // Fall-through is the normal case of a query to a real class.
3246   phi->init_req(1, query_value);
3247   region->init_req(1, control());
3248 
3249   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
3250   set_result(region, phi);
3251   return true;
3252 }
3253 
3254 //-------------------------inline_Class_cast-------------------
3255 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_Class_cast() {
3256   Node* mirror = argument(0); // Class
3257   Node* obj    = argument(1);
3258   const TypeInstPtr* mirror_con = _gvn.type(mirror)->isa_instptr();
3259   if (mirror_con == NULL) {
3260     return false;  // dead path (mirror->is_top()).
3261   }
3262   if (obj == NULL || obj->is_top()) {
3263     return false;  // dead path
3264   }
3265   const TypeOopPtr* tp = _gvn.type(obj)->isa_oopptr();
3266 
3267   // First, see if Class.cast() can be folded statically.
3268   // java_mirror_type() returns non-null for compile-time Class constants.
3269   ciType* tm = mirror_con->java_mirror_type();
3270   if (tm != NULL && tm->is_klass() &&
3271       tp != NULL && tp->klass() != NULL) {
3272     if (!tp->klass()->is_loaded()) {
3273       // Don't use intrinsic when class is not loaded.
3274       return false;
3275     } else {
3276       int static_res = C->static_subtype_check(tm->as_klass(), tp->klass());
3277       if (static_res == Compile::SSC_always_true) {
3278         // isInstance() is true - fold the code.
3279         set_result(obj);
3280         return true;
3281       } else if (static_res == Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3282         // Don't use intrinsic, have to throw ClassCastException.
3283         // If the reference is null, the non-intrinsic bytecode will
3284         // be optimized appropriately.
3285         return false;
3286       }
3287     }
3288   }
3289 
3290   // Bailout intrinsic and do normal inlining if exception path is frequent.
3291   if (too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic)) {
3292     return false;
3293   }
3294 
3295   // Generate dynamic checks.
3296   // Class.cast() is java implementation of _checkcast bytecode.
3297   // Do checkcast (Parse::do_checkcast()) optimizations here.
3298 
3299   mirror = null_check(mirror);
3300   // If mirror is dead, only null-path is taken.
3301   if (stopped()) {
3302     return true;
3303   }
3304 
3305   // Not-subtype or the mirror's klass ptr is NULL (in case it is a primitive).
3306   enum { _bad_type_path = 1, _prim_path = 2, PATH_LIMIT };
3307   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
3308   record_for_igvn(region);
3309 
3310   // Now load the mirror's klass metaobject, and null-check it.
3311   // If kls is null, we have a primitive mirror and
3312   // nothing is an instance of a primitive type.
3313   Node* kls = load_klass_from_mirror(mirror, false, region, _prim_path);
3314 
3315   Node* res = top();
3316   if (!stopped()) {
3317     Node* bad_type_ctrl = top();
3318     // Do checkcast optimizations.
3319     res = gen_checkcast(obj, kls, &bad_type_ctrl);
3320     region->init_req(_bad_type_path, bad_type_ctrl);
3321   }
3322   if (region->in(_prim_path) != top() ||
3323       region->in(_bad_type_path) != top()) {
3324     // Let Interpreter throw ClassCastException.
3325     PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3326     set_control(_gvn.transform(region));
3327     uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
3328                   Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
3329   }
3330   if (!stopped()) {
3331     set_result(res);
3332   }
3333   return true;
3334 }
3335 
3336 
3337 //--------------------------inline_native_subtype_check------------------------
3338 // This intrinsic takes the JNI calls out of the heart of
3339 // UnsafeFieldAccessorImpl.set, which improves Field.set, readObject, etc.
3340 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_subtype_check() {
3341   // Pull both arguments off the stack.
3342   Node* args[2];                // two java.lang.Class mirrors: superc, subc
3343   args[0] = argument(0);
3344   args[1] = argument(1);
3345   Node* klasses[2];             // corresponding Klasses: superk, subk
3346   klasses[0] = klasses[1] = top();
3347 
3348   enum {
3349     // A full decision tree on {superc is prim, subc is prim}:
3350     _prim_0_path = 1,           // {P,N} => false
3351                                 // {P,P} & superc!=subc => false
3352     _prim_same_path,            // {P,P} & superc==subc => true
3353     _prim_1_path,               // {N,P} => false
3354     _ref_subtype_path,          // {N,N} & subtype check wins => true
3355     _both_ref_path,             // {N,N} & subtype check loses => false
3356     PATH_LIMIT
3357   };
3358 
3359   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
3360   Node*       phi    = new PhiNode(region, TypeInt::BOOL);
3361   record_for_igvn(region);
3362 
3363   const TypePtr* adr_type = TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM;   // memory type of loads
3364   const TypeKlassPtr* kls_type = TypeKlassPtr::OBJECT_OR_NULL;
3365   int class_klass_offset = java_lang_Class::klass_offset_in_bytes();
3366 
3367   // First null-check both mirrors and load each mirror's klass metaobject.
3368   int which_arg;
3369   for (which_arg = 0; which_arg <= 1; which_arg++) {
3370     Node* arg = args[which_arg];
3371     arg = null_check(arg);
3372     if (stopped())  break;
3373     args[which_arg] = arg;
3374 
3375     Node* p = basic_plus_adr(arg, class_klass_offset);
3376     Node* kls = LoadKlassNode::make(_gvn, NULL, immutable_memory(), p, adr_type, kls_type);
3377     klasses[which_arg] = _gvn.transform(kls);
3378   }
3379 
3380   // Having loaded both klasses, test each for null.
3381   bool never_see_null = !too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_null_check);
3382   for (which_arg = 0; which_arg <= 1; which_arg++) {
3383     Node* kls = klasses[which_arg];
3384     Node* null_ctl = top();
3385     kls = null_check_oop(kls, &null_ctl, never_see_null);
3386     int prim_path = (which_arg == 0 ? _prim_0_path : _prim_1_path);
3387     region->init_req(prim_path, null_ctl);
3388     if (stopped())  break;
3389     klasses[which_arg] = kls;
3390   }
3391 
3392   if (!stopped()) {
3393     // now we have two reference types, in klasses[0..1]
3394     Node* subk   = klasses[1];  // the argument to isAssignableFrom
3395     Node* superk = klasses[0];  // the receiver
3396     region->set_req(_both_ref_path, gen_subtype_check(subk, superk));
3397     // now we have a successful reference subtype check
3398     region->set_req(_ref_subtype_path, control());
3399   }
3400 
3401   // If both operands are primitive (both klasses null), then
3402   // we must return true when they are identical primitives.
3403   // It is convenient to test this after the first null klass check.
3404   set_control(region->in(_prim_0_path)); // go back to first null check
3405   if (!stopped()) {
3406     // Since superc is primitive, make a guard for the superc==subc case.
3407     Node* cmp_eq = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(args[0], args[1]));
3408     Node* bol_eq = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_eq, BoolTest::eq));
3409     generate_guard(bol_eq, region, PROB_FAIR);
3410     if (region->req() == PATH_LIMIT+1) {
3411       // A guard was added.  If the added guard is taken, superc==subc.
3412       region->swap_edges(PATH_LIMIT, _prim_same_path);
3413       region->del_req(PATH_LIMIT);
3414     }
3415     region->set_req(_prim_0_path, control()); // Not equal after all.
3416   }
3417 
3418   // these are the only paths that produce 'true':
3419   phi->set_req(_prim_same_path,   intcon(1));
3420   phi->set_req(_ref_subtype_path, intcon(1));
3421 
3422   // pull together the cases:
3423   assert(region->req() == PATH_LIMIT, "sane region");
3424   for (uint i = 1; i < region->req(); i++) {
3425     Node* ctl = region->in(i);
3426     if (ctl == NULL || ctl == top()) {
3427       region->set_req(i, top());
3428       phi   ->set_req(i, top());
3429     } else if (phi->in(i) == NULL) {
3430       phi->set_req(i, intcon(0)); // all other paths produce 'false'
3431     }
3432   }
3433 
3434   set_control(_gvn.transform(region));
3435   set_result(_gvn.transform(phi));
3436   return true;
3437 }
3438 
3439 //---------------------generate_array_guard_common------------------------
3440 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_array_guard_common(Node* kls, RegionNode* region,
3441                                                   bool obj_array, bool not_array) {
3442 
3443   if (stopped()) {
3444     return NULL;
3445   }
3446 
3447   // If obj_array/non_array==false/false:
3448   // Branch around if the given klass is in fact an array (either obj or prim).
3449   // If obj_array/non_array==false/true:
3450   // Branch around if the given klass is not an array klass of any kind.
3451   // If obj_array/non_array==true/true:
3452   // Branch around if the kls is not an oop array (kls is int[], String, etc.)
3453   // If obj_array/non_array==true/false:
3454   // Branch around if the kls is an oop array (Object[] or subtype)
3455   //
3456   // Like generate_guard, adds a new path onto the region.
3457   jint  layout_con = 0;
3458   Node* layout_val = get_layout_helper(kls, layout_con);
3459   if (layout_val == NULL) {
3460     bool query = (obj_array
3461                   ? Klass::layout_helper_is_objArray(layout_con)
3462                   : Klass::layout_helper_is_array(layout_con));
3463     if (query == not_array) {
3464       return NULL;                       // never a branch
3465     } else {                             // always a branch
3466       Node* always_branch = control();
3467       if (region != NULL)
3468         region->add_req(always_branch);
3469       set_control(top());
3470       return always_branch;
3471     }
3472   }
3473   // Now test the correct condition.
3474   jint  nval = (obj_array
3475                 ? (jint)(Klass::_lh_array_tag_type_value
3476                    <<    Klass::_lh_array_tag_shift)
3477                 : Klass::_lh_neutral_value);
3478   Node* cmp = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(layout_val, intcon(nval)));
3479   BoolTest::mask btest = BoolTest::lt;  // correct for testing is_[obj]array
3480   // invert the test if we are looking for a non-array
3481   if (not_array)  btest = BoolTest(btest).negate();
3482   Node* bol = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, btest));
3483   return generate_fair_guard(bol, region);
3484 }
3485 
3486 
3487 //-----------------------inline_native_newArray--------------------------
3488 // private static native Object java.lang.reflect.newArray(Class<?> componentType, int length);
3489 // private        native Object Unsafe.allocateUninitializedArray0(Class<?> cls, int size);
3490 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_newArray(bool uninitialized) {
3491   Node* mirror;
3492   Node* count_val;
3493   if (uninitialized) {
3494     mirror    = argument(1);
3495     count_val = argument(2);
3496   } else {
3497     mirror    = argument(0);
3498     count_val = argument(1);
3499   }
3500 
3501   mirror = null_check(mirror);
3502   // If mirror or obj is dead, only null-path is taken.
3503   if (stopped())  return true;
3504 
3505   enum { _normal_path = 1, _slow_path = 2, PATH_LIMIT };
3506   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
3507   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
3508   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
3509   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
3510 
3511   bool never_see_null = !too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_null_check);
3512   Node* klass_node = load_array_klass_from_mirror(mirror, never_see_null,
3513                                                   result_reg, _slow_path);
3514   Node* normal_ctl   = control();
3515   Node* no_array_ctl = result_reg->in(_slow_path);
3516 
3517   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to newArray().
3518   set_control(no_array_ctl);
3519   if (!stopped()) {
3520     // Either the input type is void.class, or else the
3521     // array klass has not yet been cached.  Either the
3522     // ensuing call will throw an exception, or else it
3523     // will cache the array klass for next time.
3524     PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3525     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call_static(vmIntrinsics::_newArray);
3526     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
3527     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
3528     result_reg->set_req(_slow_path, control());
3529     result_val->set_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
3530     result_io ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
3531     result_mem->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
3532   }
3533 
3534   set_control(normal_ctl);
3535   if (!stopped()) {
3536     // Normal case:  The array type has been cached in the java.lang.Class.
3537     // The following call works fine even if the array type is polymorphic.
3538     // It could be a dynamic mix of int[], boolean[], Object[], etc.
3539     Node* obj = new_array(klass_node, count_val, 0);  // no arguments to push
3540     result_reg->init_req(_normal_path, control());
3541     result_val->init_req(_normal_path, obj);
3542     result_io ->init_req(_normal_path, i_o());
3543     result_mem->init_req(_normal_path, reset_memory());
3544 
3545     if (uninitialized) {
3546       // Mark the allocation so that zeroing is skipped
3547       AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(obj, &_gvn);
3548       alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn);
3549     }
3550   }
3551 
3552   // Return the combined state.
3553   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
3554   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
3555 
3556   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
3557   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
3558   return true;
3559 }
3560 
3561 //----------------------inline_native_getLength--------------------------
3562 // public static native int java.lang.reflect.Array.getLength(Object array);
3563 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getLength() {
3564   if (too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic))  return false;
3565 
3566   Node* array = null_check(argument(0));
3567   // If array is dead, only null-path is taken.
3568   if (stopped())  return true;
3569 
3570   // Deoptimize if it is a non-array.
3571   Node* non_array = generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(array), NULL);
3572 
3573   if (non_array != NULL) {
3574     PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3575     set_control(non_array);
3576     uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
3577                   Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
3578   }
3579 
3580   // If control is dead, only non-array-path is taken.
3581   if (stopped())  return true;
3582 
3583   // The works fine even if the array type is polymorphic.
3584   // It could be a dynamic mix of int[], boolean[], Object[], etc.
3585   Node* result = load_array_length(array);
3586 
3587   C->set_has_split_ifs(true);  // Has chance for split-if optimization
3588   set_result(result);
3589   return true;
3590 }
3591 
3592 //------------------------inline_array_copyOf----------------------------
3593 // public static <T,U> T[] java.util.Arrays.copyOf(     U[] original, int newLength,         Class<? extends T[]> newType);
3594 // public static <T,U> T[] java.util.Arrays.copyOfRange(U[] original, int from,      int to, Class<? extends T[]> newType);
3595 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_array_copyOf(bool is_copyOfRange) {
3596   if (too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic))  return false;
3597 
3598   // Get the arguments.
3599   Node* original          = argument(0);
3600   Node* start             = is_copyOfRange? argument(1): intcon(0);
3601   Node* end               = is_copyOfRange? argument(2): argument(1);
3602   Node* array_type_mirror = is_copyOfRange? argument(3): argument(2);
3603 
3604   Node* newcopy = NULL;
3605 
3606   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
3607   // the bytecode that invokes Arrays.copyOf if deoptimization happens.
3608   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
3609     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
3610 
3611     array_type_mirror = null_check(array_type_mirror);
3612     original          = null_check(original);
3613 
3614     // Check if a null path was taken unconditionally.
3615     if (stopped())  return true;
3616 
3617     Node* orig_length = load_array_length(original);
3618 
3619     Node* klass_node = load_klass_from_mirror(array_type_mirror, false, NULL, 0);
3620     klass_node = null_check(klass_node);
3621 
3622     RegionNode* bailout = new RegionNode(1);
3623     record_for_igvn(bailout);
3624 
3625     // Despite the generic type of Arrays.copyOf, the mirror might be int, int[], etc.
3626     // Bail out if that is so.
3627     Node* not_objArray = generate_non_objArray_guard(klass_node, bailout);
3628     if (not_objArray != NULL) {
3629       // Improve the klass node's type from the new optimistic assumption:
3630       ciKlass* ak = ciArrayKlass::make(env()->Object_klass());
3631       const Type* akls = TypeKlassPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, ak, 0/*offset*/);
3632       Node* cast = new CastPPNode(klass_node, akls);
3633       cast->init_req(0, control());
3634       klass_node = _gvn.transform(cast);
3635     }
3636 
3637     // Bail out if either start or end is negative.
3638     generate_negative_guard(start, bailout, &start);
3639     generate_negative_guard(end,   bailout, &end);
3640 
3641     Node* length = end;
3642     if (_gvn.type(start) != TypeInt::ZERO) {
3643       length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, start));
3644     }
3645 
3646     // Bail out if length is negative.
3647     // Without this the new_array would throw
3648     // NegativeArraySizeException but IllegalArgumentException is what
3649     // should be thrown
3650     generate_negative_guard(length, bailout, &length);
3651 
3652     if (bailout->req() > 1) {
3653       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3654       set_control(_gvn.transform(bailout));
3655       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
3656                     Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
3657     }
3658 
3659     if (!stopped()) {
3660       // How many elements will we copy from the original?
3661       // The answer is MinI(orig_length - start, length).
3662       Node* orig_tail = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(orig_length, start));
3663       Node* moved = generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::_min, orig_tail, length);
3664 
3665       // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
3666       // We know the copy is disjoint but we might not know if the
3667       // oop stores need checking.
3668       // Extreme case:  Arrays.copyOf((Integer[])x, 10, String[].class).
3669       // This will fail a store-check if x contains any non-nulls.
3670 
3671       // ArrayCopyNode:Ideal may transform the ArrayCopyNode to
3672       // loads/stores but it is legal only if we're sure the
3673       // Arrays.copyOf would succeed. So we need all input arguments
3674       // to the copyOf to be validated, including that the copy to the
3675       // new array won't trigger an ArrayStoreException. That subtype
3676       // check can be optimized if we know something on the type of
3677       // the input array from type speculation.
3678       if (_gvn.type(klass_node)->singleton()) {
3679         ciKlass* subk   = _gvn.type(load_object_klass(original))->is_klassptr()->klass();
3680         ciKlass* superk = _gvn.type(klass_node)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3681 
3682         int test = C->static_subtype_check(superk, subk);
3683         if (test != Compile::SSC_always_true && test != Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3684           const TypeOopPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->is_oopptr();
3685           if (t_original->speculative_type() != NULL) {
3686             original = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(original, t_original->speculative_type(), true);
3687           }
3688         }
3689       }
3690 
3691       bool validated = false;
3692       // Reason_class_check rather than Reason_intrinsic because we
3693       // want to intrinsify even if this traps.
3694       if (!too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check)) {
3695         Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(load_object_klass(original),
3696                                                    klass_node);
3697 
3698         if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
3699           PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3700           set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
3701           uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check,
3702                         Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
3703           assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
3704         }
3705         validated = true;
3706       }
3707 
3708       if (!stopped()) {
3709         newcopy = new_array(klass_node, length, 0);  // no arguments to push
3710 
3711         ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, original, start, newcopy, intcon(0), moved, true, false,
3712                                                 load_object_klass(original), klass_node);
3713         if (!is_copyOfRange) {
3714           ac->set_copyof(validated);
3715         } else {
3716           ac->set_copyofrange(validated);
3717         }
3718         Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
3719         if (n == ac) {
3720           ac->connect_outputs(this);
3721         } else {
3722           assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
3723           set_all_memory(n);
3724         }
3725       }
3726     }
3727   } // original reexecute is set back here
3728 
3729   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
3730   if (!stopped()) {
3731     set_result(newcopy);
3732   }
3733   return true;
3734 }
3735 
3736 
3737 //----------------------generate_virtual_guard---------------------------
3738 // Helper for hashCode and clone.  Peeks inside the vtable to avoid a call.
3739 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_virtual_guard(Node* obj_klass,
3740                                              RegionNode* slow_region) {
3741   ciMethod* method = callee();
3742   int vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
3743   assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
3744          "bad index %d", vtable_index);
3745   // Get the Method* out of the appropriate vtable entry.
3746   int entry_offset  = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset()) +
3747                      vtable_index*vtableEntry::size_in_bytes() +
3748                      vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
3749   Node* entry_addr  = basic_plus_adr(obj_klass, entry_offset);
3750   Node* target_call = make_load(NULL, entry_addr, TypePtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
3751 
3752   // Compare the target method with the expected method (e.g., Object.hashCode).
3753   const TypePtr* native_call_addr = TypeMetadataPtr::make(method);
3754 
3755   Node* native_call = makecon(native_call_addr);
3756   Node* chk_native  = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(target_call, native_call));
3757   Node* test_native = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(chk_native, BoolTest::ne));
3758 
3759   return generate_slow_guard(test_native, slow_region);
3760 }
3761 
3762 //-----------------------generate_method_call----------------------------
3763 // Use generate_method_call to make a slow-call to the real
3764 // method if the fast path fails.  An alternative would be to
3765 // use a stub like OptoRuntime::slow_arraycopy_Java.
3766 // This only works for expanding the current library call,
3767 // not another intrinsic.  (E.g., don't use this for making an
3768 // arraycopy call inside of the copyOf intrinsic.)
3769 CallJavaNode*
3770 LibraryCallKit::generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::ID method_id, bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
3771   // When compiling the intrinsic method itself, do not use this technique.
3772   guarantee(callee() != C->method(), "cannot make slow-call to self");
3773 
3774   ciMethod* method = callee();
3775   // ensure the JVMS we have will be correct for this call
3776   guarantee(method_id == method->intrinsic_id(), "must match");
3777 
3778   const TypeFunc* tf = TypeFunc::make(method);
3779   CallJavaNode* slow_call;
3780   if (is_static) {
3781     assert(!is_virtual, "");
3782     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
3783                            SharedRuntime::get_resolve_static_call_stub(),
3784                            method, bci());
3785   } else if (is_virtual) {
3786     null_check_receiver();
3787     int vtable_index = Method::invalid_vtable_index;
3788     if (UseInlineCaches) {
3789       // Suppress the vtable call
3790     } else {
3791       // hashCode and clone are not a miranda methods,
3792       // so the vtable index is fixed.
3793       // No need to use the linkResolver to get it.
3794        vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
3795        assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
3796               "bad index %d", vtable_index);
3797     }
3798     slow_call = new CallDynamicJavaNode(tf,
3799                           SharedRuntime::get_resolve_virtual_call_stub(),
3800                           method, vtable_index, bci());
3801   } else {  // neither virtual nor static:  opt_virtual
3802     null_check_receiver();
3803     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
3804                                 SharedRuntime::get_resolve_opt_virtual_call_stub(),
3805                                 method, bci());
3806     slow_call->set_optimized_virtual(true);
3807   }
3808   if (CallGenerator::is_inlined_method_handle_intrinsic(this->method(), bci(), callee())) {
3809     // To be able to issue a direct call (optimized virtual or virtual)
3810     // and skip a call to MH.linkTo*/invokeBasic adapter, additional information
3811     // about the method being invoked should be attached to the call site to
3812     // make resolution logic work (see SharedRuntime::resolve_{virtual,opt_virtual}_call_C).
3813     slow_call->set_override_symbolic_info(true);
3814   }
3815   set_arguments_for_java_call(slow_call);
3816   set_edges_for_java_call(slow_call);
3817   return slow_call;
3818 }
3819 
3820 
3821 /**
3822  * Build special case code for calls to hashCode on an object. This call may
3823  * be virtual (invokevirtual) or bound (invokespecial). For each case we generate
