3824  * slightly different code.
3825  */
3826 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_hashcode(bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
3827   assert(is_static == callee()->is_static(), "correct intrinsic selection");
3828   assert(!(is_virtual && is_static), "either virtual, special, or static");
3829 
3830   enum { _slow_path = 1, _fast_path, _null_path, PATH_LIMIT };
3831 
3832   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
3833   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInt::INT);
3834   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
3835   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
3836   Node* obj = NULL;
3837   if (!is_static) {
3838     // Check for hashing null object
3839     obj = null_check_receiver();
3840     if (stopped())  return true;        // unconditionally null
3841     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, top());
3842     result_val->init_req(_null_path, top());
3843   } else {
3844     // Do a null check, and return zero if null.
3845     // System.identityHashCode(null) == 0
3846     obj = argument(0);
3847     Node* null_ctl = top();
3848     obj = null_check_oop(obj, &null_ctl);
3849     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, null_ctl);
3850     result_val->init_req(_null_path, _gvn.intcon(0));
3851   }
3852 
3853   // Unconditionally null?  Then return right away.
3854   if (stopped()) {
3855     set_control( result_reg->in(_null_path));
3856     if (!stopped())
3857       set_result(result_val->in(_null_path));
3858     return true;
3859   }
3860 
3861   // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.  The
3862   // paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
3863   RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
3864   record_for_igvn(slow_region);
3865 
3866   // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We pull out
3867   // the vtable entry corresponding to hashCode() from the target object.
3868   // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the native
3869   // Object hashCode() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
3870   // guard for non-virtual calls -- the caller is known to be the native
3871   // Object hashCode().
3872   if (is_virtual) {
3873     // After null check, get the object's klass.
3874     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
3875     generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
3876   }
3877 
3878   // Get the header out of the object, use LoadMarkNode when available
3879   Node* header_addr = basic_plus_adr(obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes());
3880   // The control of the load must be NULL. Otherwise, the load can move before
3881   // the null check after castPP removal.
3882   Node* no_ctrl = NULL;
3883   Node* header = make_load(no_ctrl, header_addr, TypeX_X, TypeX_X->basic_type(), MemNode::unordered);
3884 
3885   // Test the header to see if it is unlocked.
3886   Node *lock_mask      = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::biased_lock_mask_in_place);
3887   Node *lmasked_header = _gvn.transform(new AndXNode(header, lock_mask));
3888   Node *unlocked_val   = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::unlocked_value);
3889   Node *chk_unlocked   = _gvn.transform(new CmpXNode( lmasked_header, unlocked_val));
3890   Node *test_unlocked  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_unlocked, BoolTest::ne));
3891 
3892   generate_slow_guard(test_unlocked, slow_region);
3893 
3894   // Get the hash value and check to see that it has been properly assigned.
3895   // We depend on hash_mask being at most 32 bits and avoid the use of
3896   // hash_mask_in_place because it could be larger than 32 bits in a 64-bit
3897   // vm: see markWord.hpp.
3898   Node *hash_mask      = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_mask);
3899   Node *hash_shift     = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_shift);
3900   Node *hshifted_header= _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(header, hash_shift));
3901   // This hack lets the hash bits live anywhere in the mark object now, as long
3902   // as the shift drops the relevant bits into the low 32 bits.  Note that
3903   // Java spec says that HashCode is an int so there's no point in capturing
3904   // an 'X'-sized hashcode (32 in 32-bit build or 64 in 64-bit build).
3905   hshifted_header      = ConvX2I(hshifted_header);
3906   Node *hash_val       = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(hshifted_header, hash_mask));
3907 
3908   Node *no_hash_val    = _gvn.intcon(markWord::no_hash);
3909   Node *chk_assigned   = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode( hash_val, no_hash_val));
3910   Node *test_assigned  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_assigned, BoolTest::eq));
3911 
3912   generate_slow_guard(test_assigned, slow_region);
3913 
3914   Node* init_mem = reset_memory();
3915   // fill in the rest of the null path:
3916   result_io ->init_req(_null_path, i_o());
3917   result_mem->init_req(_null_path, init_mem);
3918 
3919   result_val->init_req(_fast_path, hash_val);
3920   result_reg->init_req(_fast_path, control());
3921   result_io ->init_req(_fast_path, i_o());
3922   result_mem->init_req(_fast_path, init_mem);
3923 
3924   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to hashCode().
3925   set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
3926   if (!stopped()) {
3927     // No need for PreserveJVMState, because we're using up the present state.
3928     set_all_memory(init_mem);
3929     vmIntrinsics::ID hashCode_id = is_static ? vmIntrinsics::_identityHashCode : vmIntrinsics::_hashCode;
3930     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(hashCode_id, is_virtual, is_static);
3931     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
3932     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
3933     result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
3934     result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
3935     result_io  ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
3936     result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
3937   }
3938 
3939   // Return the combined state.
3940   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
3941   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
3942 
3943   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
3944   return true;
3945 }
3946 
3947 //---------------------------inline_native_getClass----------------------------
3948 // public final native Class<?> java.lang.Object.getClass();
3949 //
3950 // Build special case code for calls to getClass on an object.
3951 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getClass() {
3952   Node* obj = null_check_receiver();
3953   if (stopped())  return true;
3954   set_result(load_mirror_from_klass(load_object_klass(obj)));
3955   return true;
3956 }
3957 
3958 //-----------------inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass---------------------
3959 // public static native Class<?> sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass();
3960 //
3961 // In the presence of deep enough inlining, getCallerClass() becomes a no-op.
3962 //
3963 // NOTE: This code must perform the same logic as JVM_GetCallerClass
3964 // in that it must skip particular security frames and checks for
3965 // caller sensitive methods.
3966 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass() {
3967 #ifndef PRODUCT
3968   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
3969     tty->print_cr("Attempting to inline sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass");
3970   }
3971 #endif
3972 
3973   if (!jvms()->has_method()) {
3974 #ifndef PRODUCT
3975     if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
3976       tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because intrinsic was inlined at top level");
3977     }
3978 #endif
3979     return false;
3980   }
3981 
3982   // Walk back up the JVM state to find the caller at the required
3983   // depth.
3984   JVMState* caller_jvms = jvms();
3985 
3986   // Cf. JVM_GetCallerClass
3987   // NOTE: Start the loop at depth 1 because the current JVM state does
3988   // not include the Reflection.getCallerClass() frame.
3989   for (int n = 1; caller_jvms != NULL; caller_jvms = caller_jvms->caller(), n++) {
3990     ciMethod* m = caller_jvms->method();
3991     switch (n) {
3992     case 0:
3993       fatal("current JVM state does not include the Reflection.getCallerClass frame");
3994       break;
3995     case 1:
3996       // Frame 0 and 1 must be caller sensitive (see JVM_GetCallerClass).
3997       if (!m->caller_sensitive()) {
3998 #ifndef PRODUCT
3999         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4000           tty->print_cr("  Bailing out: CallerSensitive annotation expected at frame %d", n);
4001         }
4002 #endif
4003         return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4004       }
4005       break;
4006     default:
4007       if (!m->is_ignored_by_security_stack_walk()) {
4008         // We have reached the desired frame; return the holder class.
4009         // Acquire method holder as java.lang.Class and push as constant.
4010         ciInstanceKlass* caller_klass = caller_jvms->method()->holder();
4011         ciInstance* caller_mirror = caller_klass->java_mirror();
4012         set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(caller_mirror)));
4013 
4014 #ifndef PRODUCT
4015         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4016           tty->print_cr("  Succeeded: caller = %d) %s.%s, JVMS depth = %d", n, caller_klass->name()->as_utf8(), caller_jvms->method()->name()->as_utf8(), jvms()->depth());
4017           tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4018           for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4019             ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4020             tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4021           }
4022         }
4023 #endif
4024         return true;
4025       }
4026       break;
4027     }
4028   }
4029 
4030 #ifndef PRODUCT
4031   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4032     tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because caller depth exceeded inlining depth = %d", jvms()->depth());
4033     tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4034     for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4035       ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4036       tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4037     }
4038   }
4039 #endif
4040 
4041   return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4042 }
4043 
4044 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_conversions(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
4045   Node* arg = argument(0);
4046   Node* result = NULL;
4047 
4048   switch (id) {
4049   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToRawIntBits:    result = new MoveF2INode(arg);  break;
4050   case vmIntrinsics::_intBitsToFloat:       result = new MoveI2FNode(arg);  break;
4051   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToRawLongBits:  result = new MoveD2LNode(arg);  break;
4052   case vmIntrinsics::_longBitsToDouble:     result = new MoveL2DNode(arg);  break;
4053 
4054   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToLongBits: {
4055     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4056     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4057     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeLong::LONG);
4058 
4059     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpDNode(arg, arg));
4060     // Build the boolean node
4061     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4062 
4063     // Branch either way.
4064     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4065     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4066     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4067     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4068     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4069     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4070 
4071     set_control(iftrue);
4072 
4073     static const jlong nan_bits = CONST64(0x7ff8000000000000);
4074     Node *slow_result = longcon(nan_bits); // return NaN
4075     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4076     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4077 
4078     // Else fall through
4079     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4080     set_control(iffalse);
4081 
4082     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveD2LNode(arg)));
4083     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4084 
4085     // Post merge
4086     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4087     record_for_igvn(r);
4088 
4089     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4090     result = phi;
4091     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_long(), "must be");
4092     break;
4093   }
4094 
4095   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToIntBits: {
4096     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4097     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4098     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeInt::INT);
4099 
4100     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpFNode(arg, arg));
4101     // Build the boolean node
4102     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4103 
4104     // Branch either way.
4105     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4106     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4107     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4108     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4109     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4110     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4111 
4112     set_control(iftrue);
4113 
4114     static const jint nan_bits = 0x7fc00000;
4115     Node *slow_result = makecon(TypeInt::make(nan_bits)); // return NaN
4116     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4117     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4118 
4119     // Else fall through
4120     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4121     set_control(iffalse);
4122 
4123     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveF2INode(arg)));
4124     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4125 
4126     // Post merge
4127     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4128     record_for_igvn(r);
4129 
4130     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4131     result = phi;
4132     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_int(), "must be");
4133     break;
4134   }
4135 
4136   default:
4137     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
4138     break;
4139   }
4140   set_result(_gvn.transform(result));
4141   return true;
4142 }
4143 
4144 //----------------------inline_unsafe_copyMemory-------------------------
4145 // public native void Unsafe.copyMemory0(Object srcBase, long srcOffset, Object destBase, long destOffset, long bytes);
4146 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_copyMemory() {
4147   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
4148   null_check_receiver();  // null-check receiver
4149   if (stopped())  return true;
4150 
4151   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
4152 
4153   Node* src_ptr =         argument(1);   // type: oop
4154   Node* src_off = ConvL2X(argument(2));  // type: long
4155   Node* dst_ptr =         argument(4);   // type: oop
4156   Node* dst_off = ConvL2X(argument(5));  // type: long
4157   Node* size    = ConvL2X(argument(7));  // type: long
4158 
4159   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
4160          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
4161 
4162   Node* src = make_unsafe_address(src_ptr, src_off, ACCESS_READ);
4163   Node* dst = make_unsafe_address(dst_ptr, dst_off, ACCESS_WRITE);
4164 
4165   // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4166   // Do not let writes of the copy source or destination float below the copy.
4167   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4168 
4169   Node* thread = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
4170   Node* doing_unsafe_access_addr = basic_plus_adr(top(), thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::doing_unsafe_access_offset()));
4171   BasicType doing_unsafe_access_bt = T_BYTE;
4172   assert((sizeof(bool) * CHAR_BIT) == 8, "not implemented");
4173 
4174   // update volatile field
4175   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(1), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4176 
4177   // Call it.  Note that the length argument is not scaled.
4178   make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
4179                     OptoRuntime::fast_arraycopy_Type(),
4180                     StubRoutines::unsafe_arraycopy(),
4181                     "unsafe_arraycopy",
4182                     TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM,
4183                     src, dst, size XTOP);
4184 
4185   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(0), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4186 
4187   // Do not let reads of the copy destination float above the copy.
4188   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4189 
4190   return true;
4191 }
4192 
4193 //------------------------clone_coping-----------------------------------
4194 // Helper function for inline_native_clone.
4195 void LibraryCallKit::copy_to_clone(Node* obj, Node* alloc_obj, Node* obj_size, bool is_array) {
4196   assert(obj_size != NULL, "");
4197   Node* raw_obj = alloc_obj->in(1);
4198   assert(alloc_obj->is_CheckCastPP() && raw_obj->is_Proj() && raw_obj->in(0)->is_Allocate(), "");
4199 
4200   AllocateNode* alloc = NULL;
4201   if (ReduceBulkZeroing) {
4202     // We will be completely responsible for initializing this object -
4203     // mark Initialize node as complete.
4204     alloc = AllocateNode::Ideal_allocation(alloc_obj, &_gvn);
4205     // The object was just allocated - there should be no any stores!
4206     guarantee(alloc != NULL && alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn), "");
4207     // Mark as complete_with_arraycopy so that on AllocateNode
4208     // expansion, we know this AllocateNode is initialized by an array
4209     // copy and a StoreStore barrier exists after the array copy.
4210     alloc->initialization()->set_complete_with_arraycopy();
4211   }
4212 
4213   Node* size = _gvn.transform(obj_size);
4214   access_clone(obj, alloc_obj, size, is_array);
4215 
4216   // Do not let reads from the cloned object float above the arraycopy.
4217   if (alloc != NULL) {
4218     // Do not let stores that initialize this object be reordered with
4219     // a subsequent store that would make this object accessible by
4220     // other threads.
4221     // Record what AllocateNode this StoreStore protects so that
4222     // escape analysis can go from the MemBarStoreStoreNode to the
4223     // AllocateNode and eliminate the MemBarStoreStoreNode if possible
4224     // based on the escape status of the AllocateNode.
4225     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarStoreStore, alloc->proj_out_or_null(AllocateNode::RawAddress));
4226   } else {
4227     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4228   }
4229 }
4230 
4231 //------------------------inline_native_clone----------------------------
4232 // protected native Object java.lang.Object.clone();
4233 //
4234 // Here are the simple edge cases:
4235 //  null receiver => normal trap
4236 //  virtual and clone was overridden => slow path to out-of-line clone
4237 //  not cloneable or finalizer => slow path to out-of-line Object.clone
4238 //
4239 // The general case has two steps, allocation and copying.
4240 // Allocation has two cases, and uses GraphKit::new_instance or new_array.
4241 //
4242 // Copying also has two cases, oop arrays and everything else.
4243 // Oop arrays use arrayof_oop_arraycopy (same as System.arraycopy).
4244 // Everything else uses the tight inline loop supplied by CopyArrayNode.
4245 //
4246 // These steps fold up nicely if and when the cloned object's klass
4247 // can be sharply typed as an object array, a type array, or an instance.
4248 //
4249 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_clone(bool is_virtual) {
4250   PhiNode* result_val;
4251 
4252   // Set the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4253   // the bytecode that invokes Object.clone if deoptimization happens.
4254   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4255     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4256 
4257     Node* obj = null_check_receiver();
4258     if (stopped())  return true;
4259 
4260     const TypeOopPtr* obj_type = _gvn.type(obj)->is_oopptr();
4261 
4262     // If we are going to clone an instance, we need its exact type to
4263     // know the number and types of fields to convert the clone to
4264     // loads/stores. Maybe a speculative type can help us.
4265     if (!obj_type->klass_is_exact() &&
4266         obj_type->speculative_type() != NULL &&
4267         obj_type->speculative_type()->is_instance_klass()) {
4268       ciInstanceKlass* spec_ik = obj_type->speculative_type()->as_instance_klass();
4269       if (spec_ik->nof_nonstatic_fields() <= ArrayCopyLoadStoreMaxElem &&
4270           !spec_ik->has_injected_fields()) {
4271         ciKlass* k = obj_type->klass();
4272         if (!k->is_instance_klass() ||
4273             k->as_instance_klass()->is_interface() ||
4274             k->as_instance_klass()->has_subklass()) {
4275           obj = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(obj, obj_type->speculative_type(), false);
4276         }
4277       }
4278     }
4279 
4280     // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4281     // Do not let writes into the original float below the clone.
4282     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4283 
4284     // paths into result_reg:
4285     enum {
4286       _slow_path = 1,     // out-of-line call to clone method (virtual or not)
4287       _objArray_path,     // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_oop_arraycopy
4288       _array_path,        // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4289       _instance_path,     // plain instance allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4290       PATH_LIMIT
4291     };
4292     RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4293     result_val             = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
4294     PhiNode*    result_i_o = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4295     PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4296     record_for_igvn(result_reg);
4297 
4298     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4299     Node* array_ctl = generate_array_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4300     if (array_ctl != NULL) {
4301       // It's an array.
4302       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4303       set_control(array_ctl);
4304       Node* obj_length = load_array_length(obj);
4305       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4306       Node* alloc_obj = new_array(obj_klass, obj_length, 0, &obj_size);  // no arguments to push
4307 
4308       BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4309       if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing)) {
4310         // If it is an oop array, it requires very special treatment,
4311         // because gc barriers are required when accessing the array.
4312         Node* is_obja = generate_objArray_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4313         if (is_obja != NULL) {
4314           PreserveJVMState pjvms2(this);
4315           set_control(is_obja);
4316           // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4317           Node* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(alloc_obj, NULL);
4318           ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, obj, intcon(0), alloc_obj, intcon(0), obj_length, alloc != NULL, false);
4319           ac->set_clone_oop_array();
4320           Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4321           assert(n == ac, "cannot disappear");
4322           ac->connect_outputs(this);
4323 
4324           result_reg->init_req(_objArray_path, control());
4325           result_val->init_req(_objArray_path, alloc_obj);
4326           result_i_o ->set_req(_objArray_path, i_o());
4327           result_mem ->set_req(_objArray_path, reset_memory());
4328         }
4329       }
4330       // Otherwise, there are no barriers to worry about.
4331       // (We can dispense with card marks if we know the allocation
4332       //  comes out of eden (TLAB)...  In fact, ReduceInitialCardMarks
4333       //  causes the non-eden paths to take compensating steps to
4334       //  simulate a fresh allocation, so that no further
4335       //  card marks are required in compiled code to initialize
4336       //  the object.)
4337 
4338       if (!stopped()) {
4339         copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, true);
4340 
4341         // Present the results of the copy.
4342         result_reg->init_req(_array_path, control());
4343         result_val->init_req(_array_path, alloc_obj);
4344         result_i_o ->set_req(_array_path, i_o());
4345         result_mem ->set_req(_array_path, reset_memory());
4346       }
4347     }
4348 
4349     // We only go to the instance fast case code if we pass a number of guards.
4350     // The paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4351     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4352     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4353     if (!stopped()) {
4354       // It's an instance (we did array above).  Make the slow-path tests.
4355       // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We grab
4356       // the vtable entry corresponding to clone() from the target object.
4357       // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the
4358       // Object clone() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4359       // guard for non-virtual calls; the caller is known to be the native
4360       // Object clone().
4361       if (is_virtual) {
4362         generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4363       }
4364 
4365       // The object must be easily cloneable and must not have a finalizer.
4366       // Both of these conditions may be checked in a single test.
4367       // We could optimize the test further, but we don't care.
4368       generate_access_flags_guard(obj_klass,
4369                                   // Test both conditions:
4370                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST | JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER,
4371                                   // Must be cloneable but not finalizer:
4372                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST,
4373                                   slow_region);
4374     }
4375 
4376     if (!stopped()) {
4377       // It's an instance, and it passed the slow-path tests.
4378       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4379       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4380       // Need to deoptimize on exception from allocation since Object.clone intrinsic
4381       // is reexecuted if deoptimization occurs and there could be problems when merging
4382       // exception state between multiple Object.clone versions (reexecute=true vs reexecute=false).
4383       Node* alloc_obj = new_instance(obj_klass, NULL, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4384 
4385       copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, false);
4386 
4387       // Present the results of the slow call.
4388       result_reg->init_req(_instance_path, control());
4389       result_val->init_req(_instance_path, alloc_obj);
4390       result_i_o ->set_req(_instance_path, i_o());
4391       result_mem ->set_req(_instance_path, reset_memory());
4392     }
4393 
4394     // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to clone().
4395     set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4396     if (!stopped()) {
4397       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4398       CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::_clone, is_virtual);
4399       // We need to deoptimize on exception (see comment above)
4400       Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call, false, /* deoptimize */ true);
4401       // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4402       result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4403       result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4404       result_i_o ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4405       result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4406     }
4407 
4408     // Return the combined state.
4409     set_control(    _gvn.transform(result_reg));
4410     set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_i_o));
4411     set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4412   } // original reexecute is set back here
4413 
4414   set_result(_gvn.transform(result_val));
4415   return true;
4416 }
4417 
4418 // If we have a tightly coupled allocation, the arraycopy may take care
4419 // of the array initialization. If one of the guards we insert between
4420 // the allocation and the arraycopy causes a deoptimization, an
4421 // unitialized array will escape the compiled method. To prevent that
4422 // we set the JVM state for uncommon traps between the allocation and
4423 // the arraycopy to the state before the allocation so, in case of
4424 // deoptimization, we'll reexecute the allocation and the
4425 // initialization.
4426 JVMState* LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, int& saved_reexecute_sp) {
4427   if (alloc != NULL) {
4428     ciMethod* trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4429     int trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4430 
4431     if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4432         !C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_null_check)) {
4433       // Make sure there's no store between the allocation and the
4434       // arraycopy otherwise visible side effects could be rexecuted
4435       // in case of deoptimization and cause incorrect execution.
4436       bool no_interfering_store = true;
4437       Node* mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4438       if (mem->is_MergeMem()) {
4439         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory(), mem->as_MergeMem()); mms.next_non_empty2(); ) {
4440           Node* n = mms.memory();
4441           if (n != mms.memory2() && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4442             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4443             no_interfering_store = false;
4444             break;
4445           }
4446         }
4447       } else {
4448         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory()); mms.next_non_empty(); ) {
4449           Node* n = mms.memory();
4450           if (n != mem && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4451             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4452             no_interfering_store = false;
4453             break;
4454           }
4455         }
4456       }
4457 
4458       if (no_interfering_store) {
4459         JVMState* old_jvms = alloc->jvms()->clone_shallow(C);
4460         uint size = alloc->req();
4461         SafePointNode* sfpt = new SafePointNode(size, old_jvms);
4462         old_jvms->set_map(sfpt);
4463         for (uint i = 0; i < size; i++) {
4464           sfpt->init_req(i, alloc->in(i));
4465         }
4466         // re-push array length for deoptimization
4467         sfpt->ins_req(old_jvms->stkoff() + old_jvms->sp(), alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4468         old_jvms->set_sp(old_jvms->sp()+1);
4469         old_jvms->set_monoff(old_jvms->monoff()+1);
4470         old_jvms->set_scloff(old_jvms->scloff()+1);
4471         old_jvms->set_endoff(old_jvms->endoff()+1);
4472         old_jvms->set_should_reexecute(true);
4473 
4474         sfpt->set_i_o(map()->i_o());
4475         sfpt->set_memory(map()->memory());
4476         sfpt->set_control(map()->control());
4477 
4478         JVMState* saved_jvms = jvms();
4479         saved_reexecute_sp = _reexecute_sp;
4480 
4481         set_jvms(sfpt->jvms());
4482         _reexecute_sp = jvms()->sp();
4483 
4484         return saved_jvms;
4485       }
4486     }
4487   }
4488   return NULL;
4489 }
4490 
4491 // In case of a deoptimization, we restart execution at the
4492 // allocation, allocating a new array. We would leave an uninitialized
4493 // array in the heap that GCs wouldn't expect. Move the allocation
4494 // after the traps so we don't allocate the array if we
4495 // deoptimize. This is possible because tightly_coupled_allocation()
4496 // guarantees there's no observer of the allocated array at this point
4497 // and the control flow is simple enough.
4498 void LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_move_allocation_here(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, Node* dest, JVMState* saved_jvms,
4499                                                     int saved_reexecute_sp, uint new_idx) {
4500   if (saved_jvms != NULL && !stopped()) {
4501     assert(alloc != NULL, "only with a tightly coupled allocation");
4502     // restore JVM state to the state at the arraycopy
4503     saved_jvms->map()->set_control(map()->control());
4504     assert(saved_jvms->map()->memory() == map()->memory(), "memory state changed?");
4505     assert(saved_jvms->map()->i_o() == map()->i_o(), "IO state changed?");
4506     // If we've improved the types of some nodes (null check) while
4507     // emitting the guards, propagate them to the current state
4508     map()->replaced_nodes().apply(saved_jvms->map(), new_idx);
4509     set_jvms(saved_jvms);
4510     _reexecute_sp = saved_reexecute_sp;
4511 
4512     // Remove the allocation from above the guards
4513     CallProjections callprojs;
4514     alloc->extract_projections(&callprojs, true);
4515     InitializeNode* init = alloc->initialization();
4516     Node* alloc_mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4517     C->gvn_replace_by(callprojs.fallthrough_ioproj, alloc->in(TypeFunc::I_O));
4518     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Memory), alloc_mem);
4519     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Control), alloc->in(0));
4520 
4521     // move the allocation here (after the guards)
4522     _gvn.hash_delete(alloc);
4523     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Control, control());
4524     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::I_O, i_o());
4525     Node *mem = reset_memory();
4526     set_all_memory(mem);
4527     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Memory, mem);
4528     set_control(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Control));
4529     set_i_o(callprojs.fallthrough_ioproj);
4530 
4531     // Update memory as done in GraphKit::set_output_for_allocation()
4532     const TypeInt* length_type = _gvn.find_int_type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4533     const TypeOopPtr* ary_type = _gvn.type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::KlassNode))->is_klassptr()->as_instance_type();
4534     if (ary_type->isa_aryptr() && length_type != NULL) {
4535       ary_type = ary_type->is_aryptr()->cast_to_size(length_type);
4536     }
4537     const TypePtr* telemref = ary_type->add_offset(Type::OffsetBot);
4538     int            elemidx  = C->get_alias_index(telemref);
4539     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4540     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), elemidx);
4541 
4542     Node* allocx = _gvn.transform(alloc);
4543     assert(allocx == alloc, "where has the allocation gone?");
4544     assert(dest->is_CheckCastPP(), "not an allocation result?");
4545 
4546     _gvn.hash_delete(dest);
4547     dest->set_req(0, control());
4548     Node* destx = _gvn.transform(dest);
4549     assert(destx == dest, "where has the allocation result gone?");
4550   }
4551 }
4552 
4553 
4554 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4555 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4556 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4557 //                                                      int length);
4558 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4559   // Get the arguments.
4560   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4561   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4562   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4563   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4564   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4565 
4566   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4567 
4568   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4569   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4570   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4571 
4572   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4573   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4574   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4575   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4576   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4577   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4578   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4579 
4580   // The following tests must be performed
4581   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4582   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4583   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4584   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4585   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4586   // (6) length must not be negative.
4587   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4588   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4589   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4590 
4591   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4592   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4593   Node* null_ctl = top();
4594   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4595   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4596   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4597 
4598   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4599     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4600     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4601     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4602     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4603     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4604     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4605     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4606     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4607   }
4608 
4609   bool validated = false;
4610 
4611   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4612   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
4613   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4614   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
4615 
4616   // Do we have the type of src?
4617   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
4618   // Do we have the type of dest?
4619   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
4620   // Is the type for src from speculation?
4621   bool src_spec = false;
4622   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
4623   bool dest_spec = false;
4624 
4625   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
4626     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
4627     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
4628     // and dest so that it pays off.
4629 
4630     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
4631     bool could_have_src = has_src;
4632     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
4633     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
4634 
4635     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
4636     if (!has_src) {
4637       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4638       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
4639         could_have_src = true;
4640       }
4641     }
4642 
4643     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
4644     if (!has_dest) {
4645       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4646       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
4647         could_have_dest = true;
4648       }
4649     }
4650 
4651     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
4652       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
4653       if (!has_src) {
4654         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
4655         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4656         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4657         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
4658         src_spec = true;
4659       }
4660       if (!has_dest) {
4661         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
4662         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
4663         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
4664         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
4665         dest_spec = true;
4666       }
4667     }
4668   }
4669 
4670   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
4671     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
4672     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
4673     if (is_reference_type(src_elem))   src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
4674     if (is_reference_type(dest_elem))  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
4675 
4676     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
4677       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
4678       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
4679       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
4680       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
4681       // Do we have the exact type of src?
4682       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
4683       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
4684       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
4685       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
4686       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
4687       if (!src_spec) {
4688         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4689         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
4690           could_have_src = true;
4691         }
4692       }
4693       if (!dest_spec) {
4694         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4695         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
4696           could_have_dest = true;
4697         }
4698       }
4699       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
4700         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
4701         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
4702           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
4703         }
4704         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
4705           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
4706         }
4707       }
4708     }
4709   }
4710 
4711   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
4712   int trap_bci = bci();
4713   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
4714     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4715     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4716   }
4717 
4718   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
4719 
4720   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4721       can_emit_guards &&
4722       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
4723     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
4724     validated = true;
4725 
4726     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4727     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4728 
4729     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4730     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
4731     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
4732 
4733     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4734     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
4735 
4736     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4737     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
4738 
4739     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4740     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
4741 
4742     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4743     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
4744                          load_array_length(src),
4745                          slow_region);
4746 
4747     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4748     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
4749                          load_array_length(dest),
4750                          slow_region);
4751 
4752     // (6) length must not be negative.
4753     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
4754     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
4755     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
4756     if (EliminateAllocations) {
4757       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
4758       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
4759     }
4760 
4761     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4762     Node* src_klass  = load_object_klass(src);
4763     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
4764     Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src_klass, dest_klass);
4765 
4766     if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
4767       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4768       set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
4769       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
4770                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4771       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4772     }
4773     {
4774       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4775       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4776       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
4777                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4778       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4779     }
4780 
4781     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
4782     const Type *toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
4783     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
4784   }
4785 
4786   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
4787 
4788   if (stopped()) {
4789     return true;
4790   }
4791 
4792   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
4793                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
4794                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
4795                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
4796                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
4797                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
4798 
4799   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
4800 
4801   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4802   if (n == ac) {
4803     ac->connect_outputs(this);
4804   } else {
4805     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
4806     set_all_memory(n);
4807   }
4808   clear_upper_avx();
4809 
4810 
4811   return true;
4812 }
4813 
4814 
4815 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
4816 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
4817 AllocateArrayNode*
4818 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
4819                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
4820   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
4821   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
4822 
4823   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
4824   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
4825 
4826   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4827   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
4828   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
4829     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
4830     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
4831     return NULL;
4832   }
4833   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4834   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
4835     return NULL;
4836   }
4837 
4838   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
4839   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
4840     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
4841     if (obs != this->map()) {
4842       return NULL;
4843     }
4844   }
4845 
4846   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
4847   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
4848   assert(just_allocated_object(alloc_ctl) == ptr, "most recent allo");
4849 
4850   Node* ctl = control();
4851   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
4852     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
4853     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
4854     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
4855     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
4856       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
4857       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
4858       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
4859       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
4860         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
4861         continue;
4862       }
4863       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
4864       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
4865       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
4866       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
4867       bool found_trap = false;
4868       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
4869         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
4870         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
4871             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
4872           found_trap = true; break;
4873         }
4874       }
4875       if (found_trap) {
4876         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
4877         continue;
4878       }
4879     }
4880     return NULL;
4881   }
4882 
4883   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
4884   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
4885   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
4886   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
4887 
4888   return alloc;
4889 }
4890 
4891 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
4892 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
4893 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
4894   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
4895   // no receiver since it is static method
4896   Node *src         = argument(0);
4897   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
4898   Node *dst         = argument(2);
4899   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
4900   Node *length      = argument(4);
4901 
4902   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
4903   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
4904 
4905   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
4906   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
4907   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4908   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
4909   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
4910       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
4911     // failed array check
4912     return false;
4913   }
4914 
4915   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
4916   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
4917   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
4918   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
4919     return false;
4920   }
4921 
4922   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
4923   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
4924   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
4925   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
4926 
4927   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
4928   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
4929   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
4930   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
4931   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
4932   set_result(enc);
4933   clear_upper_avx();
4934 
4935   return true;
4936 }
4937 
4938 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
4939 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
4940   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
4941 
4942   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
4943   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
4944     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
4945   }
4946   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
4947 
4948   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
4949 
4950   // no receiver because it is a static method
4951   Node* x    = argument(0);
4952   Node* xlen = argument(1);
4953   Node* y    = argument(2);
4954   Node* ylen = argument(3);
4955   Node* z    = argument(4);
4956 
4957   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
4958   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
4959 
4960   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
4961   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
4962   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
4963   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
4964   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
4965       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
4966     // failed array check
4967     return false;
4968   }
4969 
4970   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
4971   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
4972   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
4973     return false;
4974   }
4975 
4976   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4977   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
4978   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
4979   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4980     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4981 
4982     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
4983     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
4984     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
4985     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
4986 
4987     // Allocate the result array
4988     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
4989     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
4990     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
4991 
4992     IdealKit ideal(this);
4993 
4994 #define __ ideal.
4995      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
4996      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
4997      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
4998      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
4999      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5000      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5001        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5002      } __ else_(); {
5003        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5004        sync_kit(ideal);
5005        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5006        cast->init_req(0, control());
5007        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5008        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5009 
5010        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5011        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5012        __ sync_kit(this);
5013        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5014          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5015        } __ end_if();
5016      } __ end_if();
5017 
5018      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5019        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5020        sync_kit(ideal);
5021        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5022        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5023        __ sync_kit(this);
5024        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5025      } __ end_if();
5026 
5027      sync_kit(ideal);
5028      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5029      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5030      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5031      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5032      final_sync(ideal);
5033 #undef __
5034 
5035     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5036 
5037     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5038                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5039                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5040                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5041   } // original reexecute is set back here
5042 
5043   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5044   set_result(z);
5045   return true;
5046 }

5262 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5263   address stubAddr = NULL;
5264   const char* stubName = NULL;
5265 
5266   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5267   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5268     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5269   }
5270 
5271   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5272 
5273   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5274 
5275   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5276   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5277   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5278   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5279   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5280 
5281   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5282   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5283   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5284   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5285   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5286       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5287     return false;
5288   }
5289 
5290   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5291   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5292   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5293     return false;
5294   }
5295 
5296   // Make the call
5297   {
5298     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5299     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5300 
5301     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5302                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5303                                    stubAddr,
5304                                    stubName,
5305                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5306                                    newArr_start,
5307                                    oldArr_start,
5308                                    newIdx,
5309                                    shiftCount,
5310                                    numIter);
5311   }
5312 
5313   return true;
5314 }

5360 
5361 /**
5362  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5363  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5364  */
5365 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5366   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5367   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5368   // no receiver since it is static method
5369   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5370   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5371 
5372   /*
5373    *    int c = ~ crc;
5374    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5375    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5376    *    crc = ~b;
5377    */
5378 
5379   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5380   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5381   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5382   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5383 
5384   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5385   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5386   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5387   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5388 
5389   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5390   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5391   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5392   set_result(result);
5393   return true;
5394 }
5395 
5396 /**
5397  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5398  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5399  */
5400 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5401   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5402   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5403   // no receiver since it is static method
5404   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5405   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5406   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5407   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5408 
5409   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5410   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5411   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5412     // failed array check
5413     return false;
5414   }
5415 
5416   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5417   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5418   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5419     return false;
5420   }
5421 
5422   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5423   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5424   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5425 
5426   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5427   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5428 
5429   // Call the stub.
5430   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5431   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5432 
5433   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5434                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5435                                  crc, src_start, length);
5436   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5437   set_result(result);
5438   return true;
5439 }

5441 /**
5442  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5443  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5444  */
5445 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5446   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5447   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5448   // no receiver since it is static method
5449   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5450   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5451   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5452   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5453 
5454   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5455   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5456   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5457 
5458   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5459   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5460 
5461   // Call the stub.
5462   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5463   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5464 
5465   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5466                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5467                                  crc, src_start, length);
5468   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5469   set_result(result);
5470   return true;
5471 }

5474 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_table_from_crc32c_class(ciInstanceKlass *crc32c_class) {
5475   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5476   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5477 
5478   return table;

5481 //------------------------------inline_updateBytesCRC32C-----------------------
5482 //
5483 // Calculate CRC32C for byte[] array.
5484 // int java.util.zip.CRC32C.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int end)
5485 //
5486 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32C() {
5487   assert(UseCRC32CIntrinsics, "need CRC32C instruction support");
5488   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5489   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "CRC32C class must be loaded");
5490   // no receiver since it is a static method
5491   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5492   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5493   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5494   Node* end     = argument(3); // type: int
5495 
5496   Node* length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, offset));
5497 
5498   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5499   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5500   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5501     // failed array check
5502     return false;
5503   }
5504 
5505   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5506   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5507   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5508     return false;
5509   }
5510 
5511   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5512   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5513   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5514 
5515   // static final int[] byteTable in class CRC32C
5516   Node* table = get_table_from_crc32c_class(callee()->holder());
5517   table = must_be_not_null(table, true);
5518   Node* table_start = array_element_address(table, intcon(0), T_INT);
5519 
5520   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5521   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5522 
5523   // Call the stub.
5524   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32C();
5525   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32C";
5526 
5527   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32C_Type(),
5528                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5529                                  crc, src_start, length, table_start);
5530   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5531   set_result(result);
5532   return true;
5533 }
