5656 
5657 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
5658 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
5659 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
5660   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset;
5661   guarantee(referent_offset > 0, "should have already been set");
5662 
5663   // Get the argument:
5664   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
5665   if (stopped()) return true;
5666 
5667   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
5668   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
5669   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
5670   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
5671   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
5672                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
5673                                                      false);
5674   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
5675 
5676   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
5677   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
5678 
5679   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
5680   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
5681 
5682   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
5683   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
5684   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
5685   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
5686   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
5687 
5688   set_result(result);
5689   return true;
5690 }
5691 
5692 
5693 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
5694                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
5695                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
5696   if (fromKls == NULL) {
5697     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
5698     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
5699     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
5700     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
5701     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
5702   } else {
5703     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
5704   }
5705   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
5706                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
5707                                               is_static);
5708 
5709   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
5710   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
5711 
5712   if (is_static) {
5713     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
5714     fromObj = makecon(tip);
5715   }
5716 
5717   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
5718 
5719   // Compute address and memory type.
5720   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
5721   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
5722   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
5723   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
5724   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
5725   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
5726   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
5727 
5728   // Build the resultant type of the load
5729   const Type *type;
5730   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
5731     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
5732   } else {
5733     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
5734   }
5735 
5736   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
5737 
5738   if (is_vol) {
5739     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
5740   }
5741 
5742   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
5743 }
5744 
5745 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
5746                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
5747                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
5748   if (fromKls == NULL) {
5749     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
5750     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
5751     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
5752     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
5753     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
5754   }
5755   else {
5756     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
5757   }
5758   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
5759     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
5760     is_static);
5761 
5762   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
5763   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
5764 
5765   if (is_static) {
5766     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
5767     fromObj = makecon(tip);
5768   }
5769 
5770   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
5771 
5772   // Compute address and memory type.
5773   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
5774   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
5775 
5776   return adr;
5777 }
5778 
5779 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
5780 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
5781   address stubAddr = NULL;
5782   const char *stubName;
5783   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
5784 
5785   switch(id) {
5786   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
5787     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
5788     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
5789     break;
5790   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
5791     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
5792     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
5793     break;
5794   default:
5795     break;
5796   }
5797   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
5798 
5799   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
5800   Node* src             = argument(1);
5801   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
5802   Node* dest            = argument(3);
5803   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
5804 
5805   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5806   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
5807 
5808   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5809   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5810   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
5811   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5812   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5813   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
5814 
5815   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
5816   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
5817   Node* src_start  = src;
5818   Node* dest_start = dest;
5819   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
5820     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
5821     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
5822     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
5823   }
5824 
5825   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
5826   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
5827   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
5828   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
5829 
5830   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
5831     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
5832     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
5833     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
5834     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
5835 
5836     // Call the stub.
5837     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
5838                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5839                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
5840   } else {
5841     // Call the stub.
5842     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
5843                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5844                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
5845   }
5846 
5847   return true;
5848 }
5849 
5850 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
5851 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
5852   address stubAddr = NULL;
5853   const char *stubName = NULL;
5854 
5855   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
5856 
5857   switch(id) {
5858   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
5859     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
5860     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
5861     break;
5862   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
5863     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
5864     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
5865     break;
5866   default:
5867     break;
5868   }
5869   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
5870 
5871   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
5872   Node* src                        = argument(1);
5873   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
5874   Node* len                        = argument(3);
5875   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
5876   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
5877 
5878   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
5879   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
5880 
5881   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5882   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5883   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
5884   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5885   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5886   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
5887           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
5888 
5889   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
5890   Node* src_start  = src;
5891   Node* dest_start = dest;
5892   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
5893     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
5894     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
5895     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
5896   }
5897 
5898   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
5899   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
5900   // so we cast it here safely.
5901   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
5902 
5903   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
5904   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
5905 
5906   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
5907   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
5908   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
5909   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
5910   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
5911   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
5912 
5913   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
5914   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
5915   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
5916   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
5917   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
5918 
5919   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
5920   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
5921   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
5922 
5923   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
5924   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
5925   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
5926   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
5927 
5928   Node* cbcCrypt;
5929   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
5930     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
5931     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
5932     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
5933     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
5934 
5935     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
5936     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5937                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
5938                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5939                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
5940   } else {
5941     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
5942     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5943                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
5944                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5945                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
5946   }
5947 
5948   // return cipher length (int)
5949   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
5950   set_result(retvalue);
5951   return true;
5952 }
5953 
5954 //------------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt-----------------------
5955 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
5956   address stubAddr = NULL;
5957   const char *stubName = NULL;
5958 
5959   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
5960 
5961   switch (id) {
5962   case vmIntrinsics::_electronicCodeBook_encryptAESCrypt:
5963     stubAddr = StubRoutines::electronicCodeBook_encryptAESCrypt();
5964     stubName = "electronicCodeBook_encryptAESCrypt";
5965     break;
5966   case vmIntrinsics::_electronicCodeBook_decryptAESCrypt:
5967     stubAddr = StubRoutines::electronicCodeBook_decryptAESCrypt();
5968     stubName = "electronicCodeBook_decryptAESCrypt";
5969     break;
5970   default:
5971     break;
5972   }
5973 
5974   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
5975 
5976   Node* electronicCodeBook_object = argument(0);
5977   Node* src                       = argument(1);
5978   Node* src_offset                = argument(2);
5979   Node* len                       = argument(3);
5980   Node* dest                      = argument(4);
5981   Node* dest_offset               = argument(5);
5982 
5983   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5984   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5985   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
5986   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5987   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5988   assert(top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL
5989          &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
5990 
5991   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
5992   Node* src_start = src;
5993   Node* dest_start = dest;
5994   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
5995     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
5996     src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_BYTE);
5997     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
5998   }
5999 
6000   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6001   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6002   // so we cast it here safely.
6003   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6004 
6005   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(electronicCodeBook_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6006   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6007 
6008   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6009   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(electronicCodeBook_object)->isa_instptr();
6010   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECB obj is null");
6011   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECB obj is not loaded");
6012   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6013   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6014 
6015   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6016   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6017   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6018   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6019   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6020 
6021   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6022   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6023   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6024 
6025   Node* ecbCrypt;
6026   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6027     // no SPARC version for AES/ECB intrinsics now.
6028     return false;
6029   }
6030   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6031   ecbCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF | RC_NO_FP,
6032                                OptoRuntime::electronicCodeBook_aescrypt_Type(),
6033                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6034                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, len);
6035 
6036   // return cipher length (int)
6037   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ecbCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6038   set_result(retvalue);
6039   return true;
6040 }

6042 //------------------------------inline_counterMode_AESCrypt-----------------------
6043 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_counterMode_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6044   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6045   if (!UseAESCTRIntrinsics) return false;
6046 
6047   address stubAddr = NULL;
6048   const char *stubName = NULL;
6049   if (id == vmIntrinsics::_counterMode_AESCrypt) {
6050     stubAddr = StubRoutines::counterMode_AESCrypt();
6051     stubName = "counterMode_AESCrypt";
6052   }
6053   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6054 
6055   Node* counterMode_object = argument(0);
6056   Node* src = argument(1);
6057   Node* src_offset = argument(2);
6058   Node* len = argument(3);
6059   Node* dest = argument(4);
6060   Node* dest_offset = argument(5);
6061 
6062   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6063   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6064   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6065   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6066   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6067   assert(top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL &&
6068          top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6069 
6070   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6071   Node* src_start = src;
6072   Node* dest_start = dest;
6073   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6074     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6075     src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_BYTE);
6076     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6077   }
6078 
6079   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6080   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6081   // so we cast it here safely.
6082   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6083   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6084   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6085   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6086   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(counterMode_object)->isa_instptr();
6087   assert(tinst != NULL, "CTR obj is null");
6088   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CTR obj is not loaded");
6089   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6090   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6091   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6092   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6093   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6094   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6095   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6096   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6097   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6098   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6099   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6100   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6101   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6102   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6103 
6104   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6105   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6106   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6107   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6108 
6109   Node* ctrCrypt;
6110   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6111     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6112     return false;
6113   }
6114   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6115   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6116                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6117                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6118                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6119 
6120   // return cipher length (int)
6121   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6122   set_result(retvalue);
6123   return true;
6124 }
6125 
6126 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6127 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6128 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6129   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6130   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6131   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6132   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6133   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6134   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6135   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6136     return (Node *) NULL;
6137   }
6138   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6139 #else
6140   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6141 #endif // PPC64
6142   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6143   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6144 
6145   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6146   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6147   return k_start;
6148 }
6149 
6150 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6151 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6152   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6153   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6154   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6155 
6156   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6157   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6158   return original_k_start;
6159 }
6160 
6161 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6162 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6163 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6164 // for encryption:
6165 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6166 // for decryption:
6167 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6168 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6169 //
6170 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6171   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6172   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6173 
6174   Node* src = argument(1);
6175   Node* dest = argument(4);
6176 
6177   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6178   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6179 
6180   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6181   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6182   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6183   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6184   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6185   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6186 
6187   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6188   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6189   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6190     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6191     Node* ctrl = control();
6192     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6193     return ctrl;
6194   }
6195 
6196   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6197   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6198 
6199   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6200   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6201 
6202   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6203   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6204   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6205 
6206   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6207 
6208   // for encryption, we are done
6209   if (!decrypting)
6210     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6211 
6212   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6213   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6214   // see the original java code for why.
6215   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6216   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6217 
6218   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6219   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6220   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6221   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6222 
6223   record_for_igvn(region);
6224   return _gvn.transform(region);
6225 }
6226 
6227 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6228 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6229 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6230 // for encryption:
6231 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6232 // for decryption:
6233 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6234 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6235 //
6236 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6237   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6238   Node* objECB = argument(0);
6239 
6240   // Load embeddedCipher field of ElectronicCodeBook object.
6241   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6242

6245   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object

6247   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECBobj is null");
6248   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECBobj is not loaded");
6249 
6250   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6251   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6252   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6253     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6254     Node* ctrl = control();
6255     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6256     return ctrl;
6257   }
6258   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6259 
6260   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6261   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6262   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));

6269 
6270   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6271   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6272   // see the original java code for why.
6273   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6274   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6275   Node* src = argument(1);
6276   Node* dest = argument(4);
6277   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6278   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6279   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6280   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6281 
6282   record_for_igvn(region);
6283   return _gvn.transform(region);
6284 }

6328 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6329 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {

6355                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),

6393 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6394 //
6395 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6396 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6397 //
6398 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6399 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6400 //
6401 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6402 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6403 //
6404 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6405   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6406 
6407   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6408   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6409   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6410 
6411   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6412   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6413   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6414     // failed array check
6415     return false;
6416   }
6417   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6418   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6419   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6420     return false;
6421   }
6422   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6423   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6424   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6425   Node* state = NULL;
6426   address stubAddr;
6427   const char *stubName;
6428 
6429   switch(id) {
6430   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6431     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6432     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6433     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6434     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6435     break;
6436   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6437     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6438     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6439     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6440     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6441     break;
6442   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6443     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6444     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6445     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6446     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6447     break;
6448   default:
6449     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6450     return false;
6451   }
6452   if (state == NULL) return false;
6453 
6454   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6455   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6456 
6457   // Call the stub.
6458   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6459                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6460                                  src_start, state);
6461 
6462   return true;
6463 }
6464 
6465 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6466 //
6467 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6468 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6469 //
6470 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6471   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6472          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6473   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6474   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6475 
6476   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6477   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6478   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6479   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6480 
6481   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6482   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6483   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6484     // failed array check
6485     return false;
6486   }
6487   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6488   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6489   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6490     return false;
6491   }
6492   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6493   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6494   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6495 
6496   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6497   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6498   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6499   bool        long_state = false;
6500 
6501   switch (predicate) {
6502   case 0:
6503     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6504       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6505       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6506       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6507     }
6508     break;
6509   case 1:
6510     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6511       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6512       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6513       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6514     }
6515     break;
6516   case 2:
6517     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6518       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6519       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6520       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6521       long_state = true;
6522     }
6523     break;
6524   default:
6525     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6526   }
6527   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6528     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6529     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6530 
6531     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6532     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6533     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6534     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6535 
6536     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6537     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6538     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6539     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6540   }
6541   return false;
6542 }
6543 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6544 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6545                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6546                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6547   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6548   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6549   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6550   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6551 
6552   Node* state;
6553   if (long_state) {
6554     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6555   } else {
6556     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6557   }
6558   if (state == NULL) return false;
6559 
6560   // Call the stub.
6561   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6562                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6563                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6564                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6565   // return ofs (int)
6566   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6567   set_result(result);
6568 
6569   return true;
6570 }
6571 
6572 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6573 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6574   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6575   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6576   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6577 
6578   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6579   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6580   return state;
6581 }
6582 
6583 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6584 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6585   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6586   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6587   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6588 
6589   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6590   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6591   return state;
6592 }
6593 
6594 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6595 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6596 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6597 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6598 //
6599 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
6600   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6601          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6602   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6603 
6604   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6605   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
6606 
6607   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
6608   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
6609   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
6610   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6611 
6612   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6613   switch (predicate) {
6614   case 0:
6615     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6616       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
6617       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6618     }
6619     break;
6620   case 1:
6621     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6622       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
6623       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6624     }
6625     break;
6626   case 2:
6627     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6628       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
6629       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6630     }
6631     break;
6632   default:
6633     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6634   }
6635 
6636   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
6637   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6638     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6639   }
6640   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
6641     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6642     Node* ctrl = control();
6643     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
6644     return ctrl;
6645   }
6646   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6647 
6648   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
6649   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
6650   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6651   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6652 
6653   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6654 }
6655 
6656 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
6657 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6658   Node *a = NULL;
6659   Node *b = NULL;
6660   Node *c = NULL;
6661   Node* result = NULL;
6662   switch (id) {
6663   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
6664     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
6665     // no receiver since it is static method
6666     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
6667     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
6668     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
6669     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
6670     break;
6671   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
6672     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
6673     a = argument(0);
6674     b = argument(1);
6675     c = argument(2);
6676     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
6677     break;
6678   default:
6679     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
6680   }
6681   set_result(result);
6682   return true;
6683 }

6685 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6686   // argument(0) is receiver
6687   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
6688   Node* n = NULL;
6689 
6690   switch (id) {
6691     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
6692       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
6693       break;
6694     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
6695       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
6696       break;
6697     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
6698       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
6699       break;
6700     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
6701       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
6702       break;
6703     default:
6704       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6705   }
6706 
6707   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
6708   return true;
6709 }
6710 
6711 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
6712 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6713 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
6714 
6715   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
6716   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
6717   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
6718 
6719   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
6720 
6721   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
6722     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
6723 
6724     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
6725       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
6726       return false;
6727     }
6728 
6729     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
6730 
6731     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
6732       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
6733         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
6734         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
6735       }
6736     }
6737 
6738     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
6739     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
6740     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
6741       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
6742       return false;
6743     }
6744   }
6745 */
6746 
6747   Node *a = NULL;
6748   Node *b = NULL;
6749   Node *n = NULL;
6750   switch (id) {
6751   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
6752   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
6753     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
6754     a = argument(0);
6755     b = argument(1);
6756     break;
6757   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
6758   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
6759     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
6760     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
6761     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
6762     break;
6763   default:
6764     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6765     break;
6766   }
6767   switch (id) {
6768   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
6769   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
6770   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
6771   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
6772   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
6773   }
6774   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
6775   return true;
6776 }
6777 
6778 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
6779   Node* counts = argument(1);
6780   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
6781   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
6782   if (counts->is_Con()
6783       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
6784       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
6785       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
6786     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
6787     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
6788     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
6789 
6790     if (C->log() != NULL) {
6791       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
6792                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
6793     }
6794 
6795     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
6796       // According to profile, never executed.
6797       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
6798                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
6799       return true;
6800     }
6801 
6802     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
6803     // is a number of each value occurrences.
6804     Node* result = argument(0);
6805     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
6806       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
6807       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
6808 
6809       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
6810       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
6811 
6812       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
6813       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
6814       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
6815 
6816       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
6817         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
6818         // the value has been seen at least once.
6819         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
6820         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
6821         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
6822 
6823         set_control(slow_path);
6824         set_i_o(i_o());
6825 
6826         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
6827                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
6828       }
6829       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
6830       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
6831       // later on.
6832       set_control(fast_path);
6833       result = intcon(expected_val);
6834     }
6835     // Stop profiling.
6836     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
6837     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
6838     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
6839     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
6840     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
6841     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
6842     set_result(profile);
6843     return true;
6844   } else {
6845     // Continue profiling.
6846     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
6847     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
6848     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
6849     // isn't a compile-time constant.
6850     return false;
6851   }
6852 }
6853 
6854 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
6855   Node* n = argument(0);
6856   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
6857   return true;
6858 }
